Soong Tzu-wen Expresses Urgent Desire to Raise Silver Prices 42

Plans to Submit Recommendations to the Conference

Compromise with Japan Does Not Involve Politics

(London) Chinese Finance Minister Soong Tzu-wen declared that China would join the World Tariff Truce, support genuine disarmament, and cooperate with calling countries to jointly strive to raise prices, and recognized that stabilizing silver prices is extremely important in realizing the various aspirations of the Economic Conference, and will ask the conference to set up another subcommittee to discuss the silver issue. However, although Soong guaranteed that China would join the tariff truce, he still reserved the right to notify one month in advance to stop participating. Soong stated when meeting with reporters after the Economic Committee adjourned that China could not hastily promise how much tariffs could be reduced, because the intention of Western tariffs is to protect industry, while the intention of Chinese tariffs is to generate national revenue, and the protection component is extremely small. He also said that disarmament is also an important plan to revive the economy, but the Far East will continue to be the source of anxiety in the world, due to the current relationship between China and Japan. As far as the Chinese people are concerned, they unanimously oppose Japan and its entire Far East policy. There is very little difference between Japan's political policy and military policy towards China. If the Chinese government establishes any political understanding with Japan, it may not be able to maintain its life for twenty-four hours. He has also not seen that the Chinese government will have anyone who can recognize the Japanese seizure of Manchuria. (Sixteenth National News Agency Dispatch)

(London) Chinese Finance Minister Soong Tzu-wen told a Reuters reporter today that the 50 million yuan borrowed from China by the US Financial Relief Agency is actually for the purchase of cotton and wheat, but how China uses the funds after selling the cotton and wheat is purely China's own business. The proposal of the Legislative Yuan regarding the use of loans is only an expression of opinion. Soong Finance Minister spoke about the World Economic Conference, saying that the compromise on US debts has cleared the air and slightly eased China's proposal to the Economic Committee and suggestions on white silver. He very much hoped to see the silver market stabilized and the price of silver raised. Soong Finance Minister continued to talk about the Far East, saying that China still hopes that the League of Nations will handle the Sino-Japanese dispute. The truce with Japan is limited to military affairs and not civil affairs. Any government in China that compromises with Japan and recognizes the occupation of Manchuria will definitely not be able to support it for twenty-four hours. (Sixteenth Reuters Dispatch)

Germany Decides to Postpone Debt Payments 43

75 Million Marks Extended to Next Year

Advisory Committee Asks Creditors to Reduce Interest Rates

(London) Representatives of the German government and representatives of the German National Bank met here today with the advisory committee of the creditor countries' banks and decided to revise the bad debt agreement set in 1933. The funds required by the German National Discount Bank, totaling 75 million marks, can be extended to February next year for payment. At the request of the President of the German National Bank, Schacht, the advisory committee will ask the creditors' committees of various countries to propose a reduction in the current interest rate. It has been found that the 1933 agreement was the third bad debt agreement, signed in Berlin on February 16 by representatives of 1,500 German debtors and 250 creditors from various countries, with a debt amount of approximately 370 million marks (equivalent to 180 million pounds in British gold). There are more than 6,000 debt contracts. The agreement is valid from January 1933 to the end of February 1934. Representatives from the UK, the US, France, Italy, the Netherlands, Sweden, and Switzerland all participated in the discussion at that time. In the past year, 608,000,000 marks have been issued, equivalent to 30.4 million pounds in British gold, which is 14% of the total debt under the second bad debt agreement. At the same time, the credit protected by the agreement is 378,000,000 marks, equivalent to 18.9 million pounds in British gold, which has not been used for various reasons. Now a new bad debt agreement has been established regarding German short-term loans, which reduces the average interest rate by 5%, but stipulates that the total amount of credit will be reduced by 5%. It is found that the total amount is now 260,000,000 pounds in British gold. Foreign creditors have the right to calculate and recover foreign debts borrowed from banks in Dewey marks at a rate of 50%, and recover foreign debts borrowed from the industrial sector without collateral at a rate of 30%. The funds paid according to this can be used in Germany, such as investing in real estate or mortgages or securities, and the period of this investment is at least five years. However, if the Congress believes that this kind of repayment is sufficient to endanger important national economic interests, it still has the right to veto this kind of repayment. (Sixteenth Reuters Dispatch)

(Seventeenth Electric News Agency Dispatch)

Current Commentary

Formal Announcement to the Representative of the Pacific International Studies Association from the East 45

The Fifth Annual Meeting of the Pacific International Studies Association has been decided to be held in Canada on August 14th. The topics for discussion are expected to include economic conflicts, international mediation tools and institutions for self-determination, and educational issues. Our country's representatives have already arrived in Shanghai awaiting their ship, about to embark for the meeting at a time when the Pacific Ocean is turbulent, unpredictable and changing. Representatives from various countries will, as usual, gather together and have a jovial discussion. Their peaceful and modest attitude and spirit of striving for international cooperation are truly admirable.

We still remember that the last meeting of the Pacific International Studies Association was held just after the September 18th Incident. And at this meeting, the North China Ceasefire Agreement has already been signed. This association was originally established to promote international cooperation. However, discussion is discussion, and aggression is aggression. In the year and a half since then, our country has lost millions of square miles of land, our sovereignty has been undermined, our territory has been seized, and our people have been trampled upon. Then, what is the purpose of the association's meetings and discussions? And what benefit do they bring? The answer to this question is clear without needing to be answered. I recall that at the last meeting, the association tried its best to avoid mentioning the Northeast issue. It took great pains before the meeting. Even during the meeting, few representatives from various countries spoke out for justice. This further proves that the so-called "scholars" and "celebrities" in the association all consider their national positions when advocating and arguing. They all take the interests of their own countries as the premise. The so-called fair attitude of scholars in international cooperation is just deceptive talk.

We already clearly understand the nature of the association. Therefore, we don't need to have any extravagant hopes for the association. However, as our country's representatives are about to depart, we also have to sincerely advise our representatives: (1) On this trip, you must carefully consider your own position when advocating and arguing. You must always consider the dignity of the country and the national spirit first, and you must ensure that it does not go against the will of the majority of our people. All fallacies, such as advocating waiting for fifty years to resolve the Northeast issue, or suggesting that the enemy stop military aggression and change their methods to conquer our national spirit, we sincerely hope that they will not be heard in international venues. (2) Today's international political situation is, of course, viewed differently by the benevolent and the wise, and opinions may not be entirely the same. However, the facts of the past three years are clear to the world. The aggression of the Japanese imperialists against our country is becoming more and more active. This is also something that no one can deny. The great powers are all vying with each other and only pursuing their own self-interests. The so-called international peace and international cooperation are all smokescreens to deceive weak nations. This can be seen from the active preparations for war by the great powers. We also sincerely hope that our country's representatives can recognize the current facts and not be intoxicated by the beautiful name of international scholars and make remarks that are scorned by the people of the country. (3) Do not just flaunt your fluent English and forget the essence of a certain issue. Even when discussing Chinese issues, do not speak from the perspective of foreigners and adopt a neutral attitude. All three of these are the minimum expectations we have for our country's representatives, and they are also the only expectations. The Pacific International Studies Association is responsible for "correcting the mistakes of politicians by using propaganda and education from the standpoint of scholars." However, based on the past, we do not dare to believe that the association can fulfill its responsibility.

National Government Promulgates Military Service Law 62

(Nanjing) The National Government promulgated the Military Service Law of 12 articles today, stipulating that military service is divided into national military service and regular military service. Men between the ages of 18 and 45, when not serving in the regular military service stipulated in this law, shall serve in the national military service, receive prescribed military education in peacetime, and be conscripted by order of the National Government in wartime. Regular military service is divided into compulsory service, active service, and continued service. Active service is three years, active service is six years, and continued service is filled by those who have completed their active service, and its term of service is from the date of transfer to the age of 40. The task is the same as active service. In areas where local autonomy has not been completed, the regular army may be recruited from men who are qualified by age and volunteer to serve in the military. During wartime, the term of service of each regular service may be extended. (Special dispatch on the 17th)

Public Telegram 73

Telegram from Xi'an to Shenbao and various newspapers and charitable organizations: Shaanxi's disaster is extremely severe, and the people are in danger. The spring wheat harvest is poor and there is no rain. There is a situation where it may be impossible to survive. We urgently need to provide great relief to solve the crisis. We have always admired the charitable organizations for their hard work and their repeated efforts to relieve starvation. The benevolent soup and righteous grains come from all directions. The survivors in Shaanxi are deeply grateful. But considering the current situation, we feel very embarrassed. Reports of disasters from various districts are pouring in. Based on personal observations, such as in Xingping, Wugong, Fufeng, Qishan, Fengxiang, Qian, and other districts, the summer wheat has no grains and the autumn harvest has not yet been planted. Without disaster relief and loans, and rapid planning, we fear that the delay in transportation will cause millions of lives to starve to death. The tragedy cannot be ignored. We specially telegraphed to appeal, maintain and encourage the collection of large sums of disaster relief funds to save these survivors. The disaster victims are fortunate, and all of Shaanxi is fortunate. We specially telegraphed to report and hope that you will adopt our suggestion. Zhang Ji bowed, Xian.

U.S. Congress Adjourns, Roosevelt's New Deal Plan Implemented 75

Hundreds of Thousands of People Engaged in Public Works

Aviation Bureau Builds 290 Aircraft

Washington, 16th - President Roosevelt's new plan to remedy the difficulties of the times was launched today. It is expected that it will be fully implemented within 20 days. Today, three administrative officials were specially appointed. General Johnson, a soldier, lawyer, and manufacturer, is in charge of the relief industry plan; a member of the Interstate Commerce Commission is the Federal Commissioner for Adjusting Railroads; and Colonel Sawyer, a soldier, is in charge of state construction affairs. All industries and railroads that are willing to accept federal supervision are included in the government's relief plan. The policy of comprehensive adjustment is to control overproduction and seek the existence of each individual, allowing mergers of the same industry, and thinking of cooperation and production everywhere, in order to reduce competition and eliminate waste. As for the public construction plan, 360,000 people will be engaged in afforestation and river dredging, and several million people will be engaged in house construction. Thousands of people will be engaged in building new warships and new aircraft, and 400 million yuan will be allocated to various states for road construction.

Washington, 16th - Today, Aviation Bureau Chief Major General King asked the President to include the construction of new aircraft in the public construction plan, planning to build 290 aircraft for the aircraft carriers that are about to be built. In addition, 150 aircraft will be built to replace the original aircraft that are about to be allocated to the new aircraft carrier USS Ranger. The estimated cost is more than 15 million yuan. The President immediately agreed to build 290 new aircraft, and believed that the cost of replacing the 150 old aircraft should be paid from the Navy's regular expenses.

Reuters, 16th - Washington - Before adjourning, the U.S. Congress granted great power to the President, so President Roosevelt is now practically like a dictator. The Industrial Management Act, the Bank Reform Act, and the Railroad Reorganization Act have now been signed by the President, so the number of important laws that have been implemented today is greater than on any date in American history. Roosevelt will go to the Massachusetts coast tonight and will take a yacht with his son and old friends for a half-month voyage. He plans to take the new cruiser Indianapolis to the Potomac River at the end of June at Campobello Island. It is said that if the world economy is greatly in failure at that time, President Roosevelt may take this cruiser directly to London. The Bank Reform Act has now become law and will become the largest permanent piece of legislation ever enacted by Congress. From now on, the American banking system will be actively reformed, and the various ills that have previously led to bank closures and financial turmoil may be eliminated. The Industrial Management Act stipulates 3.3 billion yuan in public

Construction project funds, and authorizes the government to implement regulations on adjusting industrial output, wages, and prices when necessary, for a period of two years.

Washington, 16th - The U.S. Congress has adjourned. Among the various emergency legislation bills, only the bill authorizing the President to ban the shipment of military supplies to belligerent countries has not been passed, because the leaders of both houses believe that there is no need to urgently pass this bill at present. In addition, there was no indication of the war debt issue in the last few days. Although Senator Johnson strongly urged the adoption of his plan to prohibit financial transactions with delinquent countries, he has not been able to get the Senate to discuss it in detail. In addition, the President's proposal to appoint non-Hawaiian residents as the governor of Hawaii was also not discussed because of the large number of opponents. Today, the U.S. President is signing the various bills that the Congress finally passed, and has signed the relief industry bill. This bill temporarily suspends the provisions of the antitrust law for industrialists and businessmen who are willing to accept government supervision. He also signed the Glass-Steagall Bank Reform Act, which prevents the use of deposits in the stock market for speculation and improves the banking system to make it more stable. He also signed the plan to reorganize the administrative agencies. This plan merges redundant agencies and reorganizes the administrative system. For example, the Office of the Commissioner of the U.S. Court for China will be transferred from the State Department to the Department of Justice. The changes will take effect in sixty days. As for the bill to reduce veterans' benefits, it is expected that the President will also sign it and announce it. This bill reduces veterans' benefits by up to 25 percent.

Washington, 16th - U.S. Agriculture Secretary Wallace announced the government's three-year grain management plan. The surtax levied on the processing and manufacturing of agricultural products first sets a standard price for the agricultural product. If the market price is lower than the standard price, a surtax will be levied according to the difference. The tax revenue will be used to subsidize farmers who reduce the number of acres planted by more than 20 percent compared to last year. For example, the standard price for wheat is set at 89 cents per bushel. The current average price is 59 cents, so a surtax of 30 cents per bushel will be levied on wheat made into flour or breakfast foods and other products, making a total of 89 cents. It is estimated that this tax will generate 150 million yuan in the first year. The management plan for cotton has not yet been announced. According to this, the surtax is only levied on sales within the country, and exports are exempt from tax in order to compete with other countries.

Havas, 17th - Washington - President Roosevelt has now departed for Massachusetts and will transfer to Maine to take a small yacht to tour the Atlantic coast for rest.

Roosevelt said, "Top European politicians, in order to break through the world crisis, advocate that there is no other way but to drive the war between Japan and the United States to create a wartime boom. All disputes should be subject to the adjudication of the International Investigation Committee." Roosevelt said, "I also agree very much. I will immediately order the authorities to investigate and study the specific case and contact Ambassador Debuchi."

The Yangtze River Water Level is Soaring 90

Chiang Orders Flood Prevention in Five Yangtze River Provinces

Breaks Sixty-Year Record

The Yangtze River Regulation Commission Urgently Seeks Disaster Prevention

The Yangtze River Water Level is Broadcasted and Reported

Beijing News. Since the beginning of summer this year, the Yangtze River has been rising day by day due to continuous rain in the upper reaches. After the torrential rain a few days ago, the Xiang River rushed down again, and the river body could not accommodate it, resulting in sudden floods and a gradual disaster. The competent authorities and the residents of the five provinces within the basin are all fearful and uneasy in light of the catastrophic events of two years ago. The Nissin News reporter specially visited Song Xishang, the director of the Engineering Department of the Yangtze River Regulation Commission, to inquire about the extent of the recent rise in the Yangtze River water level, as well as the plans for dike defense and relief. His answers are as follows:

Water Level Breaks Record. According to Song, due to budget limitations in recent years, the Yangtze River Regulation Plan could not be implemented, resulting in daily siltation of the river channel and a gradual reduction in water capacity. In the event of continuous heavy rain, it is easy to cause a rapid rise and disaster. Moreover, tracing back to the periods of high Yangtze River water levels in past years, they were all between July and August. Speaking of the 1931 flood, the Yangtze River water level in mid-June was only 39.5 feet. It later rose to 50 feet at the end of July, and soared to 53.5 feet in mid-August, causing an unprecedented disaster. However, in mid-June of this year, after the torrential rain the day before yesterday, the Yangtze River water level suddenly rose to 41 feet, which is the highest water level in the same month (June) since 1870 (61 years). If there are a little more wind and rain, it may cause a huge disaster. Moreover, this time is not the flood season. In the past, floods would inevitably occur between mid-July and mid-August, but now the water has already risen abnormally. When the flood season arrives, it will be even more worrying. It is hoped that there will be little rainfall in the future, and the water level will drop, so that the flood may be avoided.

Rapid Rise in Water Level Necessitates Flood Prevention. Song continued, the dikes of the Yangtze River have been breached for twenty years. The new dikes that have been repaired are not as strong as the old dikes. Now, considering the new dikes and the rising water levels, there are great hidden concerns. The Hubei Provincial Government and the Jianghan Engineering Bureau should be responsible for the relief and dike defense plans. However, at this extraordinary time, it seems that the two agencies are pushing responsibility to each other. As this Committee is responsible for regulating the Yangtze River, it is urging the two responsible agencies to plan and carefully prepare a plan for preventing dike disasters and providing relief to prevent future disasters. As for the height of the dikes, according to this Committee, after last year's flood, the highest water level was assumed to be 58 feet based on the extent of the flooding, and the dike body must be raised to 58 feet or more to accommodate the amount of water flowing in and combine it with the water in the heart of the river.

Broadcast Yangtze River Water Levels. Song concluded that the daily rise and fall of the water level in each port of the Yangtze River is extremely important, and it is essential that local residents and all parties fully understand this. In view of this, this Committee has specially requested the Ministry of Communications to transfer it to the Ministry of Finance, ordering the customs of each port of the Yangtze River to report the water level of that day to this Committee by special telegraph at 9:00 am every day, so that it can be reported to the Central Broadcasting Station. Since the 15th, the Shanghai, Zhenjiang, Nanjing and other customs have sent special telegrams to report the water level, which has been sent to the Central Radio Station for broadcasting. When reporting the weather, the Yangtze River water level report is added. From now on, the Central Radio Station will report the low and high tides of the Yangtze River every day. (16th)

Chiang Orders Flood Prevention in Five Provinces. Hankou Correspondence: Due to heavy rains in various places, the Yangtze River water level has continued to rise in recent days. According to the Jianghan Customs report, the water level on the 13th was 39.05 meters, 39.08 meters on the 14th, and 41.01 meters on the 15th. The upper reaches of Chongqing rose 3.9 feet in one day. The highest water level is in Wuhan, and the people are more panicked than elsewhere. After the great flood two years ago, Wuhan suffered the most severe disaster, and after the trauma, they cannot help but fear drifting. Chairman Chiang has always attached great importance to flood prevention along the river. Recently, he deemed the measures proposed by the Yangtze River Regulation Committee to be thorough and feasible. On the 14th, the Nanchang Camp sent a telegram to the National Economic Commission, the Yangtze River Regulation Committee, and the governments of the five provinces of Hunan, Hubei, Jiangxi, Anhui, and Jiangsu, instructing the seven organizations to form a Yangtze River Flood Prevention Committee. In accordance with the principle of cooperation between the central and local governments, they should work together to prevent disasters. The original telegram is disclosed as follows: "Nanjing National Economic Commission, Zhenjiang Chairman Gu, Wuchang Chairman Xia, Changsha Chairman He, Anqing Chairman Liu, Nanchang Chairman Xiong, It is said that recently, the Yangtze River volume, the coming fierce To prevent the eventuality, and to avoid repeating the same mistakes, we need to prepare flood control measures as soon as possible. We propose to form the Yangtze River Flood Control Committee, which will be jointly formed by the five provincial governments of Hunan, Hubei, Jiangxi, Anhui, and Jiangsu, the Economic Commission, and the Yangtze River Regulation Committee. The Yangtze River Regulation Committee is responsible for the matter, and all the water conservancy engineers of the seven agencies are assigned to the Yangtze River to take charge of the flood prevention work. The expenses are borne separately by the respective provincial governments and the Economic Commission, and the Central Government is asked to provide subsidies to facilitate the implementation. It is deemed feasible to establish a flood control committee jointly formed by the five provincial governments of Hunan, Hubei, Jiangxi, Anhui, and Jiangsu, the Economic Commission, and the Yangtze River Regulation Committee as requested by the Chairman. It is hoped that you will carefully consider and plan for it, and reply directly to the Yangtze River Regulation Committee for joint action." (Chiang Kai-shek (seal))" (15th)

(Reply from Hubei Provincial Government to Chiang Kai-shek). Hankou Correspondence: The Yangtze River water in Hankou rose slightly on the 16th, with the water mark reaching 41.3 feet, which is 1.9 feet higher than the water level of 39.4 feet on the same day in 1931. The rising water level in Chongqing in the upper reaches is extremely severe, rising by more than 14.8 feet in one day and night. If the Sichuan water continues to flow eastward, the situation will be more dangerous. The Hankou Headquarters has ordered the Jianghan Engineering Bureau to report the water level daily for prevention. The Hubei Provincial Government has also ordered the Bureau to rush to complete the unfinished dike project day and night to avoid repeating the mistakes of 1931. On one hand, they telegraphed Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, endorsing the proposal to jointly establish a flood control committee, saying, "We have received your telegram, stating that the Yangtze River Regulation Committee has proposed that the Yangtze River Flood Control Committee should be jointly formed by the five provincial governments of Hunan, Hubei, Anhui, Jiangxi, and Jiangsu, the Economic Commission, and the Yangtze River Regulation Committee, It is deemed feasible to plan and implement the project, and instruct you to carefully consider and plan for it, and reply directly to the Yangtze River Regulation Committee for joint action. We agree that the five provincial governments along the Yangtze River and the relevant departments in the central government should cooperate in flood prevention. " Another telegram was sent to Zhou Peizhen, Chairman of the Yangtze River Waterway Regulation Committee, saying, "We have received Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's telegram, ordering that the views of your Committee that the flood control committee should be jointly formed by the five provincial governments of Hunan, Hubei, Anhui, Jiangxi, and Jiangsu, the Economic Commission, and your Committee should be implemented. It is essential to cooperate in flood prevention in the face of the surging and severe floods. Your Committee has planned to regulate the entire Yangtze River waterway and is most familiar with the river conditions and dikes upstream and downstream. Please take charge of the implementation of appropriate measures as soon as possible. We are sending this special telegram and await your reply." As for the previous report that 48 forts in Qichun County, eastern Hubei, were breached and more than 100,000 mu of farmland were flooded, the Headquarters ordered the Provincial Government to investigate and reply, as no report had been received. The Provincial Government is now reporting to the Headquarters after receiving a report from Gu Renfa, the Administrative Inspector of the Third District and concurrently the Magistrate of Qichun County, that it is true. (16th)

Suzhou Citywide Shop Strike 91

Supporting Railway Hotel Capitalists

Suzhou Dispatch: The labor dispute at the Railway Hotel has escalated since the County Party Committee detained the hotel owner, Chen Yuting, in the police station. No resolution has been reached. After receiving reports, the central and provincial authorities successively dispatched Qi Zhiping, a member of the Central People's Movement Committee; Sheng Zhuangshu, the chief of the first section of the Provincial Secretariat; and Zhang Gongren, the chairman of the Provincial Party Headquarters, to Suzhou to investigate the situation. They have since reported their findings to the central and provincial authorities for review. On the 17th, Suzhou's various trade associations, deeming the County Party Committee's handling of the matter inappropriate, convened an emergency meeting at the Chamber of Commerce, resolving to stage a citywide strike in support of the Railway Hotel capitalists. The situation is becoming increasingly serious. The current situation is recorded as follows:

Various trade associations are deeply dissatisfied with the County Party Committee's detention of Chen Yuting, the manager of the Railway Hotel. They first convened an emergency meeting at the Chamber of Commerce on the 16th and telegraphed Chairman Chiang in Nanchang, requesting a swift and strict investigation to appease public anger. On the morning of the 17th, representatives from various trade associations gathered at the Chamber of Commerce again for a temporary emergency meeting, resolving to unanimously strike in support of Chen Yuting, the owner of the Railway Hotel. At 1:30 PM, banks on Guanqian Street and 葑門 [Fēng mén] were the first to close their doors. At 2:00 PM, money shops followed suit and ceased operations. Major stores selling silk, satin, foreign goods, and other items also closed their doors in succession, bringing a dramatic change to the bustling streets of the city. Each store displayed a piece of paper with a slogan that read: "The manager of the hospitality industry has been unjustly arrested. What dire consequences will this precedent set? We unite in support and strictly maintain order." Hotels and inns posted a separate paper that read: "The manager of the same industry has been arrested, our security is lost, and it is difficult to continue business." After receiving reports of the shop strike, the Garrison Headquarters of the Tax Police Regiment, fearing that criminals would take advantage of the situation to cause disturbances, immediately dispatched troops in vehicles to guard the Northern Bureau, the area in front of the North Temple, and the Adai Bridge outside the city to maintain order. The situation appeared tense for a time. Mao Naigong, the director of the Public Security Bureau, urgently ordered personnel from the first, second, and third branches of the city district to persuade the stores to reopen, while also dispatching patrols for strict prevention. Police units also reinforced protection near major factories. Meanwhile, the county government telegraphed the strike situation to the provincial government and the Suzhou-Changzhou Garrison Headquarters and other higher authorities.

After receiving news of the shop strike, County Magistrate Zou Xiaogong immediately summoned representatives from various labor unions, including Lu Jupo, for discussions, saying that since merchants were now taking this action, he hoped that the workers' side would remain calm and not get involved in the vortex, so as not to expand the situation, and await a central solution. The labor union representatives expressed their acceptance. Meanwhile, the Hotel Employees' Union was preparing to convene a general meeting to discuss supporting the Railway Hotel tea servers and submitted a request to the county government on the 17th for approval. County Magistrate Zou, seeing the seriousness of the current situation, advised them to postpone the meeting. Meanwhile, County Magistrate Zou and Public Security Bureau Director Mao convened a meeting with various trade associations at the County Chamber of Commerce at 5:00 PM to persuade the industries to reopen first to reassure the people. At the same time, the labor union support association also held a meeting at the County Party Headquarters to support the workers, making the situation tense.

The County Party Headquarters received repeated telephone reports at around 2:00 PM on the 17th, stating that people were distributing leaflets to various stores, urging them to close down. The County Party Headquarters immediately dispatched Gu Baiyu, a cadre, to investigate the area around Guanqian Street. He found Huang Xueshang, an employee of the Central Hotel, distributing leaflets in front of the Lilli Company, urging the closure of businesses. Gu then twisted Huang into the third branch of the second division of the Public Security Bureau and took 15 leaflets back to the Party Headquarters. Meanwhile, he sent a telegram to the county government, stating that the hospitality industry was sending people to various stores to instigate a strike, which clearly had a major impact, and requesting that personnel be dispatched for thorough investigation.

Regarding this case, in addition to receiving a report from the county magistrate here, the provincial government also sent a committee to Suzhou to investigate and report back to the province. On the afternoon of the 17th, the provincial government sent an electric order to Suzhou, the original text of which was very long. The general idea was that regarding this matter, mediation should be carried out first, and if mediation failed, arbitration should be carried out, and if arbitration was ineffective, it should be sent to the court for processing. This time, the above procedures were not followed at all, and the measures taken by the county magistrate and the director of the Public Security Bureau were improper. Moreover, the hospitality industry union had already been disbanded and was fundamentally no longer established, and it was even more inappropriate to rashly detain people based on a letter from the Party Headquarters. Now, Chen Yuting, who was detained, was to be released quickly, the county magistrate should be punished, and the director of the Public Security Bureau should be given a major demerit. After receiving the order, County Magistrate Zou immediately instructed the Public Security Bureau to release Chen, but Chen stated at the detention center of the third branch that he was unwilling to be released until the matter was resolved.

Yesterday, the 45 trade associations of the banking and money industries in Wuxian sent a circular telegram, the text of which is as follows: For the perusal of various newspaper offices, we recently sent a telegram to Chairman Chiang, the National Government, the Central Party Headquarters, the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Industry, and the Jiangsu Provincial Party Headquarters, Provincial Government, Department of Civil Affairs, and Department of Construction, stating: "The Suzhou Railway Hotel dismissed two tea waiters, and Chen Zhijun and Yan Yisheng, members of the Wuxian Party Rectification Committee, did not resolve the matter through proper channels. They suddenly arrested the manager and drove out the employees on the evening of the 12th, and sent cadres such as Xu Zishou to take over the business, which is tantamount to robbery. This sets a terrible precedent that has never been seen in Wuxian. Such rampant behavior has caused widespread panic, the law has lost its protection, and it is difficult for stores to operate. The situation is serious, and local safety is a concern. Therefore, we urgently telegraph you to quickly investigate and handle the matter to maintain public order and calm people's minds. We are extremely eager to await your orders." We hope you will investigate and publish the report to promote justice. Wuxian banking industry, money industry, pawn industry, lumber industry, north-south goods industry, and the 45 trade associations, sincerely bow. Another long-distance telephone message reported that at 7:30 PM tonight, the Wuxian County Magistrate, the Director of Public Security, and Zhang Gongren of the Provincial Party Committee convened a meeting of representatives from various trade associations at the County Chamber of Commerce. Because the representatives of various industries were angry and the order was poor, the county magistrate and others announced that each industry should select seven representatives to discuss the matter with the chairman of the Chamber of Commerce. The representatives of each industry immediately put forward three points: ㈠ Immediately dismiss Chen Zhijun and Yan Yisheng of the County Party Committee and severely punish them; ㈡ Effectively guarantee that the Party Committee will no longer illegally arrest merchants in the future; ㈢ Guarantee that Party members will no longer occupy stores in the future. The Provincial Party Committee replied: ㈠ All three requests will be submitted to the Provincial Executive Committee for resolution; ㈡ Before the provincial government decides on a solution to this case, the County Party Committee will be notified by Zhang, the Provincial Party Committee, not to act without authorization, and all parties should strictly maintain order; ㈢ The issue of reopening the market will be discussed by the Provincial Party Committee, the County Magistrate, the Director of Public Security, and the Chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, and the Chamber of Commerce will be notified. After the meeting, the 45 trade associations telegraphed the Central National Government and Chairman Chiang, requesting that Chen and Yan be dismissed. It is reported that today, representatives from the labor union also visited the County Magistrate to ask the County Magistrate to stop the strike, otherwise the labor union would also take counter-measures. In the evening, Chen Yuting, the manager of the Railway Hotel, and Huang Yunshang, who was arrested for distributing leaflets in Guanqian Street, were released. Tomorrow, except for the banks that are closed as usual due to the holiday, the money shops and merchants have decided to open for business. The troops sent to maintain order in the city were also withdrawn outside the city at 10:00 PM, and the situation has eased.

Fishing Boat Kidnapped at Jinshanwei 92

Jinshanwei, located on the coast of Punan, Songjiang, has a resident named Yang Zhengqing who owns a fishing boat. The other day, the boat owner suddenly received a report stating that one of the fishing boats had an accident in the outer sea. Pirates in a boat emerged from a certain mountain bay and robbed Yang's fishing boat as it passed by. The boat had few valuable items, so they took the boat's captain and first mate onto their pirate boat, raised the sail, and fled. It is learned that the boat owner is currently investigating the whereabouts of the fishing boat. The boat has not yet returned, and it is unknown whether it will return safely.

Manufacturer of Poison Pills Escorted to the Province 93

Cao Guozhen, the chief surgeon of Tongren Hospital in Wuxi, and three others, including Tu family seller Zhu Zongyuan and Zhao Benli, jointly established a large-scale poison pill manufacturing organization inside the destroyed Ruisheng Silk Cocoon Warehouse under the Gongyun Bridge in the county. The Fourth Branch of the Jiangyin Drug Investigation Team discovered the matter and dispatched personnel to arrest them. They arrested Zhang Yanbin and three other accountants, along with the stolen goods, and escorted them to Cheng. However, the main culprits, Cao Guozhen, Zhu Zongyuan, and others, escaped and fled to Shanghai. Later, a Mr. Wei went to Cheng to bail out Zhang Yanbin in order to track down the main culprits. However, after Zhang's release for half a month, the main culprits were still not found. Yesterday, Director He dispatched personnel to arrest Zhang in Cheng and sent him along with the stolen goods to the Zhenjiang General Office for legal action.

Tax Police Chief Investigates Commercial Port Boundary 94

The Ministry approved the establishment of a commercial port within a specified boundary. However, the opening of the commercial port in Xiyi took place between 1922 and 1923, when Yang Shounan was the director. Although he actively promoted it, and the Ministry appointed a boundary demarcation committee in 1924, the demarcation was not implemented due to local opposition and frequent political turmoil. The boundary has not been finalized due to numerous obstacles. As a result, disputes have frequently arisen with old salt merchants. Subsequently, the Fine Salt Company submitted a request that was approved by the Executive Yuan, stating that the prosperous roads around the outer city of Xiyi, from Jingyun in the east to Kaiyuan in the west, were all areas for the sale of fine salt. The company then expanded its business to the surrounding countryside, and the salt sales decreased, leading to renewed disputes over the boundary. The other day, Zhang Zhongli, the chief of the Songjiang Salt Affairs Inspection Branch of the Tax Police Bureau, specially accompanied salt merchant representatives Lu Zhongdan and Luo Yangxuan, as well as Yan Dayong, the chief of the sixth district stationed in Changzhou, Wang Yusheng, the chief of the branch stationed in Xiyi, and Wu Hanzhuang, the inspector-general of the Changzhen district, along with patrol captains Liu Yunlong and Wang Wenhai, to Xiyi. They contacted the chiefs of each district through the sixth branch of the Public Security Bureau and went to the commercial port area to investigate the boundary. Director Zhang also invited County Magistrate Yan and representatives from both the traditional salt merchants and the fine salt company to a meeting at the County Chamber of Commerce yesterday (the 17th) morning. The fine salt company did not send representatives to attend because the sales area had already been stipulated by an order from the Executive Yuan, making further discussion unnecessary. As a result, Director Zhang decided to submit the commercial port boundary map, the opinions expressed in writing by Shuangli, and the proposals of the Chamber of Commerce to the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Finance and Industry for approval.

Jiangyin Ship Robbed 95

The regular ferry boat from Changzhou's Wuyi to Jiangyin loaded goods and passengers in Changzhou around 7:00 PM on the 16th and set sail for Jiangyin. At around 9:00 PM, when it arrived at the Cangtou Bridge, it was suddenly robbed. The passengers' hidden money and belongings were all stolen. The boat returned after the incident and docked at the Jiangyin pier outside the North Gate. On the 17th, they went to the Shipping Association to request reporting the case to the authorities.

Anti-Japanese Association Seizes Large Batch of Anti-Japanese Yarn 96

The Wuyi Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association recently received a tip-off that the Qi Zhengyan Lihua Cotton Weaving Factory was purchasing a large batch of anti-Japanese yarn in Shanghai, which would be delivered to the factory soon. At around 5:00 AM on the 16th, the inspectors took a car to the factory and found more than 200 packages of unlicensed anti-Japanese yarn in the factory's warehouse. They then received another tip-off that a cargo ship had sailed east in an attempt to escape, so they immediately tracked it down. After chasing it for about seven miles, they intercepted the ship and found 15 pieces of Liuma brand anti-Japanese yarn. They ordered it to return to the factory, and then took the factory's accountant, Lin Youe, and more than 800 packages of anti-Japanese yarn back to the city. They convened an emergency meeting and decided to value the seized anti-Japanese yarn and impose penalties in accordance with regulations. If the accountant Lin Youe has a reliable shop guarantor, he will be allowed to be released.

Labor Dispute at Changfeng Cloth Factory Escalates 97

The Changfeng Cloth Factory outside the Shuibeimen Gate in Changshu has been very successful in its business, but it is very harsh on its female workers. They work from 6:00 AM to 6:00 PM every day, which makes the female workers resentful. The other day, the factory heavily punished and ordered a female worker named Gu Yueyuan to weave more cloth because she had woven damaged cloth, which aroused the anger of the female workers, who agreed to strike. They went to the Public Security Branch Office in the jurisdiction to report that they were being oppressed by the factory and requested relief and a reduction in working hours. The police officers from the branch office went to mediate, and the factory was willing to reduce the working hours, and the female worker Gu Yueyuan was also willing to resign voluntarily, and the matter was settled. Both parties agreed to implement the agreement on the 16th, but unexpectedly, the factory suddenly went back on its word and insisted on suspending the employment of several people who had led the strike, which led to another strike. The female workers had a firm attitude and settled accounts with the factory after measuring the dimensions and amounts of cloth. When the Public Security Bureau heard the news, they went to mediate again, but the factory was also willing to close down because the cloth sales were sluggish. Both sides went to extremes, and the disturbance became more serious.

Loving Mother Strangles Her Child 98

Wu Ni, a widow in the Changshou Temple area of the Tenth District, is nearly thirty years old and has a graceful appearance. Unwilling to live alone, she repeatedly considered remarrying, but she had an eight-year-old son named A'er who was very foolish. Fearing that he would be a burden in the future, she had long planned to kill him. After dinner on the 14th of this month, Ni strangled A'er to death with a rope. Fearing that she would be suspected, she placed the body upside down in a chamber pot. She remained calm, locked the door, and went out to work in the fields. When she returned home in the evening, she pretended to be sad and told her neighbors that her son had died in the chamber pot. The neighbors did not suspect anything at first and deeply lamented. Unexpectedly, when the body was being prepared for burial the next day, the rope marks on the neck were obvious, and the news spread throughout the neighborhood. It is now reported that the county government will send someone to examine the body.

Yangtze River Police Bureau Abolished 99

The Zhenjiang Yangtze River Police General Bureau was previously ordered by the General Headquarters to temporarily close down, and the police branches in various provinces were to remain under the control of the respective provincial governments. Six of the eight ships previously transferred from the Ministry of Navy were returned, leaving two ships specifically for anti-smuggling matters. It is heard that the chief of the Jiangsu Provincial Branch received instructions yesterday.

Militia Dies in Action Against Bandits 101

The Rushi Zhuangwan militia of Rugao received a secret report the other day (the 13th) that Zhang Kuilong, a notorious bandit from Taixing, had secretly come to Shi and was plotting wrongdoing. He was hiding in the home of Zhang Songtao in Shaobazhuang. Eight militiamen were dispatched to search the area, but unexpectedly, there were as many as nine bandits hiding there. The bandits were alerted when the militiamen arrived and immediately drew their weapons and resisted. The militiaman Zhou De'an bravely stepped forward, but the magazine of his box-type gun was jammed and malfunctioned. The bandits fired a barrage of bullets, hitting Zhou in the left chest and right abdomen, and he fell to the ground and died. The bandits took the opportunity to flee. The regional militia has reported the incident to the county for examination.

Breached River Embankment Repaired by Rushing to Block 102

The river embankment in the Langshan area of Nantong, Nantong, was breached by a large tide for more than a hundred zhang. The tide poured in. The embankment protection association has raised a large sum of money to hire workers to rush to repair and block the breach. Meanwhile, Xu Ji of the Provincial Committee designed an embankment protection project and submitted it to the provincial government, requesting funding according to the precedent of the Jiangnan Pond project.

Case of Squad Leader Murdered Solved 103

Wang Zhongxin, a squad leader of the Second Police Squad of Jingjiang (previously mistakenly reported as Wang Zongxing), was shot and killed near Dongwai Hengqiao. County Magistrate Chen Guiqing paid close attention to the case. On the 14th night, Wang Zhongxin's usual gun was found on the South Street Bridge next to the Zhaoshang Hotel. Xu Longzi reported this to the county government. County Magistrate Chen believed that there was a clue to be found, so he secretly interrogated the four squad leaders who had been with Wang Zhongxin that day, Guo Yanjun, Xue Dalong, Gao Xingfa, and Wang Xicai. They confessed that at 3:00 AM on the morning of the 12th, Guo Yanjun had arranged with Xue Dalong, Gao Xingfa, and Wang Xicai to lure Wang Zhongxin to Dongwai. Xue Dalong and others first knocked Wang Zhongxin to the ground, and Guo Yanjun took Wang Zhongxin's box-type gun and fired three shots at his head, killing him. The perpetrators have been shackled and imprisoned, and Yang Kongshi has also been captured and sent to the county for legal action.

Robbery Occurs in Daixi Township 104

A pirate ship with more than a dozen bandits on board suddenly arrived at Daixi Township in Hubei's Huzhou Prefecture at around 9:00 PM the other day. They stormed ashore, broke into the home of a farmer named Tong Yinchu in the township, and stole seven carts of raw and processed silk, more than thirty pieces of clothing and bedding, and more than ten yuan in cash. By the time the town's Public Security Bureau heard the news and led police officers to pursue them, they were gone. The victim, Tong Yinchu, and his neighbor, Guo Jinlian, fled to the roof of their house. The bandits spotted them and fired a pistol, causing them to lose their footing and fall to the ground, severely injuring them.

Four Battalion, Company, and Platoon Leaders Executed by Firing Squad 105

In September of last year, the Zhejiang Security Brigade received a complaint from Pan Tianzheng and others in Ninghai County, accusing Ji Liang, the battalion commander of the First Battalion of the Fifth Regiment of the Ninghai Security Brigade, of corruption, embezzlement, and illegally collecting opium taxes. A secret order was issued to the regiment and the county to conduct a detailed investigation. Later, the case was shelved because the person involved in the case, Platoon Leader Yang Guozhen, fled to avoid punishment and was wanted but not found. In March of this year, Yang Guozhen suddenly changed his name to Yang Zhicai and came to Hangzhou in disguise, still seeking a job with the Security Department, thus walking into a trap and being detained. He confessed that in May of last year, Battalion Commander Wei Liang sent Adjutant Hu Nai, Company Commander Liao Tingfan, and other private individuals to various areas to investigate opium seedlings. The village chiefs requested exemption from taxation because the opium seedlings were ready for harvest. After negotiations, the village chiefs issued five promissory notes totaling about four or five hundred yuan and handed them to his private individuals to take back to the battalion headquarters. Later, when a secret investigation committee from the provincial government arrived in the county, all opium seedlings had to be eradicated. Fearing that the public would object, Ji Liang sent the promissory notes to the village chiefs through Yang Yingshi, the company clerk. The Security Department reported the incident and immediately telegraphed the Fifth Regiment to suspend Battalion Commander Ji Liang, Company Commander Liao Tingfan, and former Adjutant Hu Nai, who was now the Company Commander, and jointly escort them, along with Yang Yingshi, the company clerk, and squad leader Feng Zairong, who were also involved in the case. A military court was organized for trial, and they confessed without hesitation. It was determined that Ji Liang and others were all incumbent military officers who dared to condone the planting of opium poppies and demand promissory notes, which was an unforgivable crime. According to the provisions of the Army, Navy, and Air Force Criminal Law and the Zhejiang Province Provisional Regulations for Eradicating Drugs of the Republic of China Criminal Law, they were sentenced to death. At 9:00 AM yesterday (the 17th), the Security Department sent personnel to execute Battalion Commander Ji Liang, Company Commander Hu Nai, Liao Tingfan, and Platoon Leader Yang Zhicai by firing squad. Yang Yingshi and Feng Zairong were acquitted and released.

To Treat Old Ailment

Nanjing Telegram: Wang Jingwei, accompanied by Zeng Zhongming, traveled to Shanghai by special train No. 1 at 11:00 PM on the 17th to treat an old ailment and visit Chen Bijun, who is ill. He is scheduled to disembark at Zhenru tomorrow morning.

Sun Ke Discusses the Progress of the Sino-American Loan 107

Central Telegram Orders Song Ziwen to Proceed

Hu Hanmin Misunderstands and Sends Telegram for Explanation

Sun Ke, the president of the Legislative Yuan, received reporters from various newspapers at his residence on Columbia Road yesterday morning and spoke about the various issues of the Sino-American loan and its uses. Mr. Sun first stated that Song Ziwen was proceeding with this Sino-American loan based on the intentions of the Central Government. After Song's departure from the country, the National Defense Committee convened a meeting to discuss China's specific plans for the Washington Conference. Public opinion felt that China's agricultural and forestry economy was on the verge of collapse, which had a significant impact on the national economy, people's livelihood, and the world economy. It was necessary to take emergency measures to provide relief. Therefore, it was decided to instruct Song to seek material assistance from the United States to revive China's economy. After Song received the order and consulted repeatedly in the United States, the cotton and wheat loan was finally established.

Regarding the use of cotton and wheat, Mr. Sun continued to say that this American cotton and American wheat loan was originally a short-term credit loan, which was completely different from the nature of ordinary foreign debt. The regulations for American cotton stipulate that within three months of the arrival of the goods in China, one-tenth of the price must be paid first, and the rest will be repaid in installments. In the future, the proceeds will be used to develop the Northwest and construct transportation and water conservancy. The Legislative Yuan submitted and passed the Sino-American Loan Agreement yesterday (the 16th) and resolved to organize a Loan Management Committee to avoid waste. However, the details of the organization and the allocation of personnel must be decided by the Central Political Conference.

Mr. Hu's Misunderstanding Mr. Hu Zhantang, who resides in Hong Kong, has a lot of misunderstandings about the Sino-American loan and has telegraphed me to express his opposition. Mr. Hu's reasons are: First, this loan is Mr. Song's personal action and has not been passed by the Legislative Yuan; second, past domestic debts have been consumed in civil wars, and the establishment of this Sino-American loan may lead to another outbreak of civil war, and the Legislative Yuan should deny it. I have now telegraphed Mr. Hu in detail to explain that this loan is based on the principles set by the Central Government and is not Mr. Song's personal action. The Legislative Yuan is responsible to the Central Government. Since this loan is the intention of the Central Government, it is certainly not illegal. I continued to say that this loan will be used for construction and production and will absolutely not be consumed in civil wars. If it can be carefully managed, it will certainly not be wasted. The Legislative Yuan has resolved to organize a Loan Management Committee to prevent waste, and it has now been submitted to the Central Political Conference for adoption.

Economic Conference The London Economic Conference focuses on the United Kingdom, the United States, and France, and China has less involvement. Recently, the United States has experienced a surplus of agricultural products, low prices, weak purchasing power of farmers and workers, and more than ten million unemployed people. This is the contradiction of capitalism, so the United States has adopted a policy of currency inflation to seek relief. France advocates restoring the gold standard, while the United Kingdom advocates setting a rigid exchange rate first and then restoring the gold standard in the future. Each country has different interests and different opinions. China advocates raising the price of silver and stabilizing the price of silver. Stabilizing the price of silver benefits all countries and is expected to be adopted. Mr. Song is expected to return to the country around the end of July or the beginning of August.

Review of the Draft Constitution Mr. Sun finally stated that the first draft of the Constitution has now been completed and is being reviewed. We have contributed many opinions. It has now been decided to submit the first draft to the subcommittee for review first, then to the Constitution Drafting Committee for discussion, and then to the Legislative Yuan for passage before submitting it to the Central Political Conference for approval. In the future, it will be submitted to the National Assembly for passage in the name of the Central Executive Committee, and the Constitution will be formally established.

Yesterday's Salary Increase Movement for Clerks and Staff on the Two Railways 108

The Authorities Did Not Reply Yesterday

Resolution Expected After Requesting Instructions

The clerks and staff of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways have not yet received their annual salary increases for the twenty-second year, and recently there have been rumors that the annual salary increases will be canceled. The clerks and staff of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway specially established the "Representatives' Congress for the Salary Increase Movement for the Twenty-Second Year of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway Traffic Staff" in Wuxi on the fifteenth. The next day, they telegraphed the authorities, requesting a satisfactory response within forty-eight hours. The clerks and staff of the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway also convened a representatives' congress in Jiaxing on the sixteenth, unanimously responding. In addition to telegraphing their sympathy to their colleagues on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway, they also telegraphed the authorities for a definite reply. The news obtained yesterday is recorded below:

Shanghai-Hangzhou Responds Acknowledging with respect your telegram from the Wuxi Beijing-Shanghai Railway Traffic Staff Representatives' Congress for the Salary Increase Movement for the Twenty-Second Year. The annual salary increase concerns the vital interests of our colleagues. Having resolved, we express our deep sympathy and earnestly hope that you continue to fight and keep us informed at any time. First Representatives' Congress Presidium, Shanghai-Hangzhou Section Branch Office, bowed, Xian.

We, the colleagues of our factory, vow to provide full assistance and wholeheartedly support it. Sixth Branch of the Wusong Machine Factory Branch Office, Colleagues of the Materials Factory, Qia.

Telegraph Inquiry to the Authorities To the Director and Traffic Director of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration: The annual salary increase is divided into two periods per year. The first period is about to end, and the second period will follow. We have already submitted a request, but there has been no good news. The masses are anxiously awaiting. What progress has the railway administration made on this issue? Please provide a definite reply to dispel doubts. First Representatives' Congress Presidium, Shanghai-Hangzhou Section Branch Office, bowed, Xian.

Request for Instructions Submitted to the Ministry Regarding the clerks' and staff's request for annual salary increases, the two railway administrations have submitted a request to the Ministry of Railways for instructions on how to handle it. Director Huang Boqiao also met with Minister of Railways Gu Mengyu in Shanghai on the fourteenth of this month to request instructions. At the same time, considering the seriousness of the situation, Police Chief Yuan Boyang was dispatched to Beijing by night train on the fifteenth to contact the Ministry of Railways and report on the progress.

Notice to Clerks and Staff Director Huang Boqiao and Deputy Director Wu Shaozeng gathered the heads and deputy heads of the General Affairs, Engineering, Traffic, Materials, Mechanical, and Accounting departments at 2:00 PM on the sixteenth to explain the handling of this matter and instructed them to inform their subordinates that there was no intention to cancel the salary increase. They have already requested instructions from the Ministry. At the same time, they announced to the clerks and staff in the two railways' daily publications, saying, "Regarding the employee salary increase issue this year, this administration has requested the Ministry to give instructions and has dispatched Deputy Director Yuan to the Ministry for contact. An official order will be issued soon."

The Administration's Statement The secretariat of the two railway administrations declared to the Xin Xin News Agency reporters yesterday that Article 5 of the "Regulations on Salary for National Railway Staff" revised and promulgated by the Ministry on May 30th, 1920, stipulates, "The promotion of staff and clerks requires a record of merit from the previous rank or promotion, which can be submitted by the administration to the Minister of Railways for approval to advance one level." This administration has decided to handle it in accordance with the regulations. Since the clerks and staff telegraphed requesting a response within a time limit, the administration has requested instructions from the Ministry and will handle it after the Ministry's order. However, it is hoped that employees will not engage in any unfortunate incidents.

Clerks' and Staff's Attitude The total number of employees under the two railway administrations is about 13,000. The annual salary increases for workers in the twenty-second year were implemented in January of this year. There are about 400 clerks and staff in the administrative offices. Since requesting the railway administration to reply within a time limit, Xin Xin News Agency reporters met with clerks and staff of the Traffic Department yesterday. According to them, the 48-hour deadline will expire on the morning of the 18th. Before the deadline expires, the clerks and staff will not express anything for the time being. However, it is hoped that the railway administration will give a satisfactory response to meet the expectations of the public.

Final Solution The reporters from the Guowen News Agency later obtained news from other sources that the salary increase movement representatives telegraphed the authorities to give a satisfactory response within 48 hours, which is due this morning (18th). The Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo section established a similar organization yesterday, and there will soon be an expression. As for the final steps if the clerks and staff do not get a satisfactory response, it is heard that because the workers have already been increased, there is no problem. Vehicles will still run as usual, and all the clerks and staff on the railway will implement not selling tickets, allowing guests to ride at will. Although in a slowdown, traffic is still not interrupted. Yesterday, the two railway administrations' party headquarters held a regular meeting and raised a discussion on this, but the content was confidential and unknown.

Extension of Response The Traffic Department clerks and staff of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways requested annual salary increases for the twenty-second year and telegraphed the two railway administrations, requesting a satisfactory response within 48 hours. The railway administration has submitted a request to the Ministry of Railways for instructions on how to handle it. According to a certain source, the 48-hour deadline started on the morning of the sixteenth and expires this morning. However, the railway administration believes that it needs to request instructions from the Ministry of Railways, and it is impossible to reply in such a short period due to the exchange of official documents. A special representative was sent to guide the clerks and staff, requesting an extension to Tuesday (20th), and there will be a satisfactory response. The clerks and staff have indicated acceptance and are waiting for a solution. Also, Minister of Railways Gu Mengyu returned to Beijing by night train yesterday. When reporters met him on the train, they asked about his attitude towards the railway administration clerks and staff's request for a salary increase. Gu did not want to express anything at that time. (Central News Agency)

Hankou River Water Rises Again 109

Xi Dejiong Flew to Hankou Yesterday for Active Defense

The Shanghai National Economic Commission's Engineering Office received a report from the Jianghan Engineering Bureau yesterday that at 12:00 noon on the 17th, the water level in Hankou was 41 feet 8 inches, which is 5 inches higher than yesterday, which is shocking. Fortunately, the sky has cleared since the 16th, and the water may decrease slightly from now on. The Economic Commission has allocated a huge sum of money to the Jianghan Bureau to purchase defense tools such as hemp bags, lead wires, and water piles, and deploy them in sections for defense. Also, Engineering Office Director Xi Dejiong was approved to fly to Hankou on the afternoon of the 17th to supervise the bureau and actively defend it.

French Tea Expert Goubeaux Comes to China for Investigation 110

| Japanese Tea Dumping in the Philippines, French Merchants Attach Importance |

| Goubeaux Offers Suggestions to Improve Chinese Tea |

Our country's red and green tea leaves shipped to various African territories reach millions of taels per year. Since Japan began shipping green tea to that area the year before last, it has suddenly increased by two million pounds in three years. It also promoted that Chinese tea contains various toxins and directly dumped tea at low prices to consumers. Not only was the sale of Chinese tea in the Philippines greatly affected, but French merchants in Africa were also panicked. In order to understand whether the tea produced in China is as bad as the Japanese claim, and the intention of the Japanese propaganda in the Philippines, the merchants specially requested the French government to send personnel to China for investigation. The investigation commissioner Goubeaux (Jean Goubeau) dispatched by the French government arrived in Shanghai last month. Goubeaux is a French agricultural engineer and has worked as a tea master at the Annam Agricultural Research Institute for more than ten years. He is very familiar with the tea industry in the East. After arriving in Shanghai, he and Fan Hejun, a translator assigned by the French Consul, went to Zhejiang, Anhui, Jiangxi, and the two lakes to investigate tea-producing areas. After returning to Shanghai a few days ago, he visited Cai Wuji, Director of the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau of the Ministry of Industry, and Wu Juenong, the tea inspection technician of the bureau, regarding the improvement of the methods of transporting and planting Chinese tea in the Philippines. The two parties discussed it four or five times. According to the person in charge of the inspection bureau, Goubeaux believes that banning colored tea and gathering strength to promote it externally are the fundamental ways to save Chinese tea. When he arrived in Qimen, Anhui, he visited the Anhui Provincial Tea Improvement Farm. He also praised the farm's success in handling sales cooperation this year and its policies on experimental planting methods. In this city, he will visit several tea merchants before planning to go to Japan for investigation.

Cotton and Grain Industry Association's Opinion on Cotton and Wheat Loans 111

Matters Concerning People's Livelihood Should Be Considered Comprehensively

The Shanghai Cotton and Grain Industry Association submitted a letter to the Central Government, the Executive Yuan, the Legislative Yuan, and the Ministry of Industry, addressed to Director Song. "The news that Minister Song signed a contract in the United States to borrow a huge sum of 50 million for cotton and wheat has shocked the country. We have been reading your speeches in the newspapers for days. The loan contract has been established, and you have prepared measures and submitted them to the Yuan. We admire your comprehensive planning. However, the total amount of the loan is 50 million US dollars, and it is stipulated that four-fifths will be used to purchase cotton and one-fifth to purchase wheat and flour. The contract content, such as procurement prices, shipping, and distribution, is up to Minister Song to consider, which is profound and unpredictable. However, this matter is of great importance and relates to the livelihood of the entire people. The association operates in the cotton industry and is familiar with the situation, and there are several points that we cannot help but speak out. We humbly present them to you, Director. Our country is based on agriculture, and its agricultural products are the best in the world. Only because of endless internal strife and frequent droughts and floods, planting is not timely, and famine often occurs. To save it, we should eliminate private views, unite sincerely, quell internal unrest, rectify agricultural production, and improve planting to enrich people's livelihood. Borrowing money to live is not a long-term plan. This is one. The bankruptcy of agricultural villages affects social stability. In recent years, grain prices have fallen, farmers have abandoned their fields and scattered in all directions. Even suicides in ditches have been reported in newspapers from time to time. The number of vagrants has surged in large cities, which is a great social concern. Revitalizing agricultural villages is an urgent task today. If foreign surplus agricultural products are used to oppress dying farmers, the hope of revival will eventually be in vain. Foreign countries dump their products, and cash is depleted. Major powers promote domestic products, mostly limiting imports. The United States prohibits the import of cotton products, which is clear evidence. However, the dumping continues, coupled with huge loans, which is tantamount to the government becoming a sales agency for foreign merchants, creating opportunities for friendly countries' products, and giving strong neighbors the excuse to import. The leakage is huge, and the national system is concerned. This is two. The total output of domestic cotton is about 8 million dan on average. If we can do our best to promote it and improve it, with our country's suitable land, the yield will definitely increase. According to past output, it is more than enough to supply our country's self-operated yarn factories. Even in the event of a famine, the difference is not much, and manufacturers can purchase it themselves. Moreover, yarn sales have been stagnant to the extreme in recent years. Since hearing the rumors of the huge loan, the market price of cotton yarn has fallen sharply within a week. If a huge amount of foreign cotton is imported, the value of domestic cotton will inevitably be even worse than today. The disadvantages are not only that cotton prices will be cheaper and cotton farmers will be directly harmed, but also that yarn stocks will be thicker and yarn merchants will find it difficult to support. This is four. In the past, yarn manufacturer Rong Zongjing spread the rumor of borrowing cotton from the United States, and the public was panicked and asked to stop it. Since receiving instructions, public doubts have been dispelled. The brilliant instructions, the ink is not dry, the impact of small loans to individuals on society has been extremely significant, let alone those who are more than this. The advantages and disadvantages of this are self-evident. This is five. In summary, based on the evidence of our country's products and the current situation, it seems that there is no need to accept this loan from the United States, whether it is cotton or wheat flour. We humbly ask for your opinion to follow public opinion and withdraw the order. In the event that it is inconvenient to change due to international credibility, the signing of a formal contract must be carefully planned, with the premise that it does not hinder domestic products, and then make suggestions. And beg to approve the line, one cotton price average, cotton is a major domestic product, the people's livelihood concerns, accounting for about five-sixths of the people, American cotton prices should be based on the average of the historical Sino-American cotton prices, two procurement knowledge, about the quality of raw materials, must be familiar with, China and the United States cotton producing areas production, domestic yarn factories' supplies produced in and social needs, take the shared strengths, complement our shortcomings, only in order to make the most of it, use all the amount of three things rare is expensive, the surplus is waste, then shipping should pay special attention to, if you can divide a long time, to the rest of his state, make up for our lack of, supply and demand, perhaps the shortcomings, if in a short period of time, the entire batch is shipped, then supply exceeds demand, cotton prices, the situation is suppressed, must anticipate the lack of real, shipped in batches, no backlog, four distribution issues, is even more important, the newspaper reported that the Minister of Industry said, if the distribution is not its law, then it will not only be of no help to us, that the inherent domestic cotton industry yarn industry will also suffer its extremely bad influence, Zhizai Siyan, sincere and essential, our country's own yarn factories, the total number of eighty-four, the annual cotton, the average per plant to seventy thousand dan, but six million dan, in addition to the application of domestic cotton, the lack of limited, nearly because yarn sales dismal, the implementation of reduced labor, then the required raw materials, more and more reduced, so to distribute this huge amount of American cotton, must recruit sophisticated British Chamber of Commerce and Others Suggest Silver Price and Commodity Prices Must Increase Proportionately 113

Otherwise It Will Be Harmful to China's Export Trade

The Zi Lin News reported that the joint committee of the British Chamber of Commerce and the China Association in this city telegraphed the headquarters in London, the British Overseas Trade Bureau, and the Federation of Industries yesterday (16th), stating that artificially raising the price of silver without a corresponding increase in commodity prices will harm Chinese trade. The telegram claimed that the joint committee of the British Chamber of Commerce and the China Association passed a resolution today, which stated that stabilizing the price of silver tends to increase trade, but if artificially raising the price of silver without a corresponding increase in world commodity prices will greatly reduce China's export trade, limit its purchasing power, and cause serious financial difficulties for China, which may lead to the abolition of the single list, which will be very harmful to Chinese trade.
