Wang Delin's Department Arsenal Director Yu Junqing Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday Morning 116

Detailed Account of the Unit's Anti-Japanese and Russian Retreat Experience

Only by Continuing the Anti-Japanese War Can We Repay the People

Yu Junqing, the director of the arsenal of Wang Delin's troops, the Commander-in-Chief of the Jilin National Salvation Army, arrived in Shanghai from Hong Kong yesterday morning. A Far East News Agency reporter specially visited him to inquire about the details, which are recorded as follows:

(Anti-Japanese Experience) Since the September 18th Incident, Yu Junqing, acting as the director of the Jilin Province, witnessed the humiliation of the invasion by a strong neighbor. Believing that everyone is responsible for the rise and fall of the world, he participated in the anti-Japanese work and was entrusted by Commander Wang to serve as the director of the arsenal. After several months of fierce fighting, the strong enemy was frightened. At that time, all the supplies of equipment and bullets were planned by the factory. When the Ma Zhanshan troops lost, our army was threatened, so we had to retreat from Dongning, Jilin to Shuangchengzhi in Russia on January 13th this year (Wang Kong Avoided Russia). An emergency meeting was convened to gather the entire army, and everyone requested that Commanders Wang (Delin) and Kong (Xianrong) enter Russia temporarily to preserve their strength. They set off from Shuangchengzhi on the 24th and arrived in Domsk on March 11th. The subordinate troops were reorganized and remained in Jilin Province, lurking in various places, adopting the Russian guerrilla strategy of the Russian-Japanese War in 1918. On April 14th, they set off from Domsk to Poland.

(Arrived in Poland) They arrived in Bodi on the 19th, and the local overseas Chinese warmly welcomed and comforted them, and gave many gifts. Commander Wang expressed his gratitude and declined. Cheng set off for Berlin on that day, departed from Berlin on the 27th, arrived in Geneva, Italy on the 28th, and arrived in Hong Kong on the 5th of this month on the Sapolikin vehicle.

(Guangdong and Macau Welcomed) When arriving in Hong Kong, more than 3,000 people from various institutions and groups in Guangdong Province and the people of the city welcomed him and firmly invited him to visit the province. Commanders Wang and Kong could not refuse the kindness, and accompanied the representatives of the province to visit the province on the same day.

(Coming to Shanghai Soon) After arriving in the province, they originally planned to stay for a while and then come to Shanghai. Later, because all sectors of Macau sent representatives to welcome them, they could not refuse and stayed in Macau for at most one or two days before returning to Hong Kong and transferring to Shanghai.

(Continuing the Anti-Japanese War) I and Senator Xu Jiesan took the Taikoo Company's Suzhou wheel on the 12th and came to Shanghai first to take care of everything. Once Commanders Wang and Kong arrive in Shanghai, if there are any other delays, they should go to the front line immediately, lead the troops to continue the anti-Japanese war, recover the lost land, to fulfill their long-cherished wishes, and to repay the people.

Original Country Mark of Imported Goods is Allowed to be Changed to Original Country Text 117

Customs Superintendent Tang Haian and Tax Officer Berlede jointly issued Bulletin No. 1306 yesterday to change the text of the original country name marking of imported goods. It is hereby announced that the regulations on the marking of the original country name of imported goods stipulate that imported goods should be marked with the original country name in Chinese characters, which was announced on February 8th of this year. If there are difficulties in marking the above-mentioned goods in Chinese characters, it should be allowed to be marked with the original country text to facilitate it. It is hereby announced to all merchants, etc.

The Tiachu Monosodium Glutamate Factory has joined the International Safety Association, so it specially initiated the organization of the Industrial Safety Association in this city. On the sixth of last month, it convened the first meeting of initiators and elected fifteen members of the preparatory committee, which held three preparatory meetings. There are now more than thirty member groups (ie factories) and more than ten individuals. The case has been filed with the Party and government agencies and will be officially established today. The purpose of this association is to seek the safety of factory equipment and reduce the danger of workers. The business of this association includes the research, design, and guidance of factory hygiene and other facilities, the inspection of safety equipment entrusted by member factories, and the improvement of health conditions, the popularization of knowledge of industrial safety and industrial hygiene, and other matters related to the safety of industry that should be handled. In the future, members of this association should work together.

The failure of our country's industry is due to the failure to improve and stick to the old ways. In the future, we should strive for innovation, so that not only can workers enjoy safety, but also the industrial future has great hope. Then Wu Liguo, the representative of Li Tingan, gave a speech, saying that I represent the Health Bureau and am deeply gratified by the establishment of your bureau. In the future, this bureau is willing to do its best for the equipment and improvement plans of industrial hygiene.

How should this association promote the implementation of the industrial safety movement? Resolved, handed over to the board of directors for handling. 3. Continue to solicit members. Resolved, handed over to the board of directors for handling. 4. Publish publications. Resolved, the publication is named "Industrial Safety", and the first issue is scheduled to be published on July 1.

It was resolved to meet at the temporary office before 2:30 PM next Monday. 3) Drafting a relocation plan. Special Aviation News 124

Jianghan Customs Cracks Down on River Pilots: After the establishment of the Yangtze River Pilots Association, the Yangtze River pilots currently employed by various ships are required to register with the association and obtain licenses. Otherwise, they are not allowed to practice. However, there are still many unlicensed pilots employed by various river vessels. In order to ensure safe navigation, approval has been obtained from the Ministry of Communications and the Ministry of Navy to implement a crackdown on unlicensed "wild chicken" pilots, starting with the Jianghai Customs, which will strictly restrict them. Starting on the 16th of this month, Jianghai Customs specifically issued a notice that all Chinese and foreign ships must submit their pilot's license for verification when departing from Hankou. If the pilot does not have this license, the customs clearance will be immediately stopped, and the ship will not be allowed to depart. After the promulgation of this new regulation, river vessels generally have to rehire licensed pilot personnel. On the first day of the new regulation's promulgation, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Jianghua and Jiangjing vessels were departing from Hankou. Although their pilots had licenses, they were in Shanghai and had not brought them with them to Hankou. They were almost prohibited from customs clearance by Jianghan Customs. Only after repeated proof were they allowed to sail. Yesterday, various shipping companies in Shanghai received telegrams from Hankou reporting that unlicensed pilots can no longer practice on the Yangtze River, informing various river vessels to replace them as soon as possible, otherwise, it is feared that it will affect the shipping schedule.

Taigu Sends Personnel to Study Navigation: Many graduates from the Wusong Merchant Marine School have been hired by domestic shipping companies as senior officers. Their performance has even surpassed that of foreign officers. In order to save expenses, the British Taigu Steamship Company has recently gradually hired senior Chinese officers for its Yangtze River vessels to replace Westerners. They have also been working very hard in their duties. Now, the Taigu authorities have gone a step further and decided to select personnel to study at the Wusong Merchant Marine School. Fearing that the school will not admit them, they specifically requested to add auditors so that they can be sent to the school to study various navigation subjects together. This matter has been entrusted to our aviation community to discuss with Principal Xu Zufan. Once it is determined, Taigu will immediately send personnel to the school.

South Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway Gates Stations Rented Out 129

Monthly Rent, Can Still Be Recovered at Any Time

Central News Agency reports that the two-way Railway Bureau, in order to handle responsible transportation, followed the order of the Ministry of Railways to take back the freight yards and warehouses that were occupied or rented out at the South Gate and South Star stations, first one after another, for future use. Recently, the Xieji Yonghuitong, Dafeng, Anyu, Daji, and Jinqu Paper Industry Guilds at the South Gate, and the Fuyang County Grass Paper Industry Association, and all paper merchants jointly submitted a request, stating that most of the bulk grains and paper goods transported by the South Gate and South Star stations are produced in various townships in Jinqu and Yushanli Mountain in Fuyang. Due to the wind and waves of the Qiantang River, they must be gathered at the two stations and reported in batches. Since the railway bureau took back the freight warehouses, it has been difficult to select and sort them. They requested consideration of the merchants' difficulties and requested that the freight warehouses still be rented out to benefit both parties. After the Traffic Department found that the location of the freight warehouses at the two stations was still spacious and that customers were directly reporting and transporting without congestion, and that if merchants could not rent warehouses, it would also be inconvenient to rent houses outside the warehouses to stack goods. According to the regulations in Section 7 of Article 5 of the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo line freight car transportation rules, it is permissible to rent them out. The rental price will be revised, and it is stipulated that they will be rented on a monthly basis, so that they can be recovered at any time when the goods are congested.

Page 14

The truth of the Wei Tingrong case has come to light

Zhao Weishen Declared Not Guilty 132

丨The Garrison Headquarters Announced the Judgment Yesterday丨

Wei Himself Instigated the Kidnappers to Falsely Accuse Zhao Weishen and Was Also Involved

The Truth Was Revealed in the Confessions of the Bandits, and There Are Records Available in the Second Special Court

In the case of Wei Tingrong, the former Commander-in-Chief of the Chinese Volunteer Army in the French Concession, who was kidnapped in 1929, five criminals, Cai Weicai, Lü Ruowang, Zhu Jingcheng, Chen Zhongheng, and Tang Shiliang, were successively apprehended. Among them, Zhu, Chen, and Tang were sentenced to five years of imprisonment by the former French Mixed Court. After serving their terms, they were still handed over to the Chinese mainland authorities for further handling. Cai and Lü were sentenced to death by the Second Special District Court in 1931, which was later commuted to life imprisonment by amnesty. However, there was still a suspect in the case, Zhao Weishen, who was identified by the bandits as the mastermind behind the case. Zhao and Wei Tingrong were actually brothers-in-law, both being sons-in-law of the late gentry Zhu Baosan. When Zhao Weishen was accused of being the mastermind of the kidnapping, he was working in the former Ministry of Finance's Revenue Police Corps. The court, considering him to be an active-duty soldier, ordered him to be handed over to the military law office for trial. The police department disagreed and appealed, but the original judgment was upheld. The police department disagreed again and appealed again, but the result of the three trials was still to uphold the original judgment. Therefore, Zhao Weishen was recently transferred to the military law office of the Garrison Headquarters. The military law office immediately opened a court to interrogate Zhao. Zhao vehemently protested his innocence, stating that he had absolutely nothing to do with the case and that he was being falsely accused by the bandits. Therefore, the military law office summoned the four criminals, Zhu, Chen, Tang, and Cai, to confront him. According to the joint confession of Zhu, Cai, and Chen, they had indeed falsely accused Zhao Weishen, and the person who instigated the false accusation was Wei Tingrong. According to Zhu Jingcheng, when he was arrested, he suffered gunshot wounds and was lying in the hospital. Wei Tingrong personally came to the hospital and instructed him to falsely accuse a certain prominent figure and Zhao Weishen as the masterminds. If he was willing to comply, Wei would do his best to find a way to get him acquitted and would also cover his son's education expenses until he graduated from university. At first, Quan Chu did not agree, but then Wei came three more times. Moved by profit and influence, he falsely accused Zhao Weishen. However, in the end, Wei went back on his word and never tried to get him acquitted, merely using him as a tool to take revenge for his personal grudges, which was not worth it. Now, his conscience has awakened, so he is telling the truth according to the circumstances. Recently, Qian Lihe, a rickshaw puller, was also arrested in the case. When the Second Special Court opened the trial after his capture, Zhu had already fully confessed the above situation, and there are records available for verification. The military law office then obtained the records of the confessions of the criminals from the Second Special Court, interrogated them repeatedly, and as a result, concluded that there was insufficient evidence to prove Zhao Weishen's guilt and declared him not guilty. The full text of the judgment of the Garrison Headquarters is transcribed below:

Copy of the Judgment of the Songhu Garrison Headquarters "Judgment" Defendant Zhao Weishen, 32 years old, from Yanling County, Hunan Province, Battalion Commander of the Independent Sixth Battalion of the Revenue Police Corps of the Ministry of Finance. The above defendant was transferred to this department by the Third Branch of the Jiangsu High Court for trial on suspicion of kidnapping and extortion. The judgment is as follows: "Main Text" Zhao Weishen is not guilty. "Facts" On July 24, 1929, a case of Wei Tingrong being kidnapped by bandits occurred on Avenue Edward VII (i.e., Zhubao San Road) in this city. The French police arrested three accomplices, Zhu Jingcheng (Zhu Fengxiang), Chen Zhongheng (i.e., Wang Kui), and Tang Shiliang (i.e., Tang Wenchun), who were sentenced separately by the former French Mixed Court and sent to prison. Later, in 1931, the French police successively arrested two accomplices, Cai Weicai (i.e., Jin Fuming) and Lü Ruowang (i.e., Qian Fangxiang), in this city. Zhao Weishen, a suspect, was arrested in Suzhou and brought to the Shanghai Second Special District Court for trial. After the court's investigation, Lü Ruowang was sentenced to life imprisonment and Cai Weicai was sentenced to 20 years of imprisonment. Zhao Weishen was deemed to be an active-duty soldier and was sentenced to be tried by military law. At that time, the French police department declared its disagreement with the part of the Zhao Weishen case that was transferred to military jurisdiction and appealed to the Third Branch of the Jiangsu High Court, which rejected the appeal. Subsequently, Zhang Zongru, the prosecutor of the court, declared his disagreement and appealed to the Supreme Court, which rejected the appeal on January 7 of this year. Once the case was finalized, the Third Branch of the High Court sent the complete file and the defendant Zhao Weishen to this department. "Reasons" The defendant Zhao Weishen was identified by the plaintiff Wei Tingrong and the French police in August 1931 as the mastermind behind the kidnapping and extortion, and a public prosecution was filed. Later, due to disputes over jurisdiction, an appeal was made to the Supreme Court, which finally decided to transfer the case to this department for trial. After the case was brought for interrogation, the defendant firmly denied participating in the kidnapping. After reviewing the original file of the Second Special District Court, it was found that the plaintiff Wei Tingrong stated in his complaint that the mastermind of the case, Zhao Weishen, was identified by the arrested criminals Cai Weiran (referring to Cai Weicai) and Lü Ruowang, and requested the court to send detectives to investigate. Furthermore, the prosecution document of the French police department on August 21, 1931, stated that Zhao Weishen was identified by the arrested people (referring to Chen Zhongheng and Lü Ruowang) as the mastermind in the kidnapping of Wei Tingrong, and requested that he be investigated and dealt with in accordance with Article 371 of the Criminal Law. It is clear that the purpose of the prosecution in this case was to exclusively adopt the statements of Cai, Chen, Lü, etc., as testimonies. Furthermore, after reviewing the trial records of Chen's file on August 28 and November 24 of the same year, no corresponding testimony from Cai Weicai was found. In summary, the testimonies of Lü and Chen are summarized below: ㈠ Lü Ruowang confessed that after Wei was kidnapped, in the seventh lunar month (the exact date is unclear), I went to the Chengzhan Hotel in Hangzhou with Chen Zhongheng and Zou Juen to send a letter, and the Wei family handed over 1,000 yuan. After returning, Zou, Chen, and I went to the rooftop garden of the Wing On Company and met Zhao Weishen. Zou introduced us, saying that Zhao and Wei were brothers-in-law, and that Zhao was the one who kidnapped Wei. He also said that Zhao had said he wanted to kidnap Wei. ㈡ Chen Zhongheng confessed that Zou Juen first asked Lü Ruowang to borrow 200 yuan from me, but he did not repay it when it was due. Soon, Zou and Lü came to my house and invited me to meet Zhao Weishen at the rooftop garden of the Wing On Company. Zhao said at the time that Wei Tingrong was wealthy but unkind, embezzled public funds from the Volunteer Army, and was unrighteous, so he wanted to kidnap him. Four or five days later, I went to Hangzhou to see the exhibition and met my brothers Zou and Lü. Because I had heard about the kidnapping at the Wing On Garden, I was more eager to collect the debt. The next day, Lü invited me to the Chengzhan Hotel to get it, and I heard him negotiate the kidnapping with the Wei family. I left first (the rest is omitted). After carefully examining the above confessions, the times when the criminals met with the defendant do not match. One said it was after returning from Hangzhou, and the other said it was before going to Hangzhou. Which is right and which is wrong cannot be determined. Moreover, both criminals confessed that Zhao said he wanted to kidnap Wei. The meaning of the words proves that he had not yet started to commit the crime, and in fact, the plaintiff had already been kidnapped. Therefore, this testimony is not credible. Moreover, the defendant is an active-duty mid-level military officer and is not foolish. Even if he had criminal intentions, he would never easily talk about it to a friend he had just met. Furthermore, the confessions of Lü and Chen are vague and cannot be regarded as reliable evidence. Since this case was transferred to this department for trial, the plaintiff Wei Tingrong has not been summoned for investigation of the facts. Later, it was reported that he no longer intends to pursue the defendant. Furthermore, the court approved the document sent by the Third Branch of the High Court on May 30, informing us of the recording of the group to the department. After checking, there is a statement by lawyer Fei Xizhen of the Police Department of the French Concession, which briefly stated that the current police department has investigated and found that the defendant Zhao Weishen has no criminal suspicion, and regarding the public prosecution part, they are willing to withdraw the prosecution and request the presiding judge to directly release the defendant. Based on this observation, since the plaintiff has declared that he has abandoned his right to sue, and the original prosecuting agency has requested to withdraw the public prosecution, the foundation of the defendant's crime has been destroyed. It should be considered that the right to sue has been extinguished. Furthermore, after investigating the reasons for the defendant's counterclaim, it was briefly stated that he had a relationship with the plaintiff through marriage, and because they were both running the Volunteer Army in the French Concession, the plaintiff was jealous and did not hesitate to instigate the criminals in his kidnapping case to falsely accuse him. Zhu Jingcheng, Cai Weicai, Chen Zhongheng, and Tang Shiliang (another person named Lü Ruowang was reportedly sent to Anhui by the court and could not be brought back) were brought to the case for interrogation. According to Zhu, Chen, Cai, etc., Wei Tingrong did teach us to bite Zhao Weishen four times and lured us with candies and other things, promising to reduce our sentences. Furthermore, the Shanghai Second Special District Court sent the original file of Qian Lihe, a suspect recently arrested in this case, to the department. After reviewing the trial record of May 29 of this year, the previous situation confessed by the criminals was recorded in detail. Based on this verification, it can be seen that the defendant's counterclaim is also well-founded. In summary, since the defendant's criminal suspicion is insufficient, a verdict of not guilty should be given in accordance with the provisions of Article 316 of the Code of Criminal Procedure. The judgment is as follows: Commander Dai Ji, Military Law Office Director Wang Yizhe, Military Judge Yu Shiyun, Clerk Guo Tingyuan, June 15, 1933, Republic of China

The Supreme Court Ordered a Retrial of the Zhang Wenqing Matricide Case 133

The Police Department Appealed to the Supreme Court

It Has Been Delayed for Two Years

丨Yesterday, Everyone Changed Their Testimony at the Retrial丨

Zhang Wenqing, the daughter of the late Huzhou native Zhang Fusheng, who once served as a county magistrate, conspired with Chen Hengcai, the son of her family's female servant Chen Wang, to kill her mother, Zhang Su, because she resented her mother's control over the inheritance. On January 25, 1930, Chen Hengcai, along with his cousin Yao Yonggui and fellow villager Gao Jintang, took a sharp pocket knife from home and went to Zhang's house at 762 Carter Road, stabbing Zhang Su in the neck. Chen and others immediately fled, while Zhang Wenqing reported the robbery to the police afterward. When Zhang Su was sent to the hospital by the police, Zhang Wenqing also went to the hospital under the guise of inspecting, taking the opportunity to take away the deposit certificate of 2,000 taels from the Xingye Bank, the deposit certificate of 400 yuan from the Great World Day and Night Bank, and 45 yuan in cash that Zhang Su was carrying. Later, Zhang Su died of her injuries. After the police found out the truth, they arrested Zhang Wenqing and other men and women and filed a public prosecution for the crime of conspiracy to commit murder. On June 17 of that year, the Shanghai Special District Court sentenced Zhang Wenqing and Chen Hengcai to death for the crime of instigating murder, and Yao Yonggui and Gao Jintang to death for the crime of conspiracy to commit murder. The criminals were not satisfied and hired lawyers to appeal to the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court. After investigation by the court, except for Chen Hengcai, who was sentenced to death according to the original judgment, the other three, Zhang Wenqing and others, were sentenced to life imprisonment. However, the criminals still expressed dissatisfaction with the judgment of the second instance and appealed to the Nanjing Supreme Court. Wang Zhennan, the chief prosecutor of the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court, and the Shanghai Municipal Council of the Public Concession believed that the second instance's abandonment of the original death sentence for the three criminals Zhang Wenqing, Yao Yonggui, and Gao Jintang and the change to life imprisonment was too lenient, so they also appealed to the Supreme Court, requesting that the original judgment of the first instance be upheld. This appeal has been going on for two and a half years, and the Supreme Court has not yet announced the final judgment. Therefore, although Zhang Wenqing and others are imprisoned separately in men's and women's prisons, they are still treated as prisoners awaiting trial. However, Yao Yonggui died of illness in prison last year due to ineffective medical treatment. Now, the Supreme Court believes that the judgment of the second instance still has some unclear points and specifically instructed the Second Branch of the High Court, saying that the case has room for investigation in all aspects, and the case is complex. It is difficult to clarify the truth without careful investigation. The original trial was too hasty to be convincing. The original judgment should be revoked and sent back for a new trial. Yesterday morning, Yu Ye, the presiding judge of the criminal court of the Second Branch of the High Court, and Zhao and Jiang, the two judges, and the prosecutor and clerk, went to the First Criminal Court and ordered the three criminals Zhang Wenqing and others to be brought to the case. Gan Jingxian, the lawyer of the Police Department, Wang Chuanbi, Zhang Wenqing's defender, Fan Gang and Fan Qisheng, Chen Hengcai's defender, and Wu Zhiping, Gao Jintang's defender, all appeared in court one after another. The judge questioned the three criminals one by one. Unexpectedly, Zhang Wenqing and others overturned and denied most of the confessions in the first and second trials, denying that they had instigated or conspired to murder Zhang Su. Although they were repeatedly questioned by the court, they all denied it in one voice. After the lawyers debated with each other, the official announced that the case would be sentenced on June 24. Zhang Wenqing and others were still sent back to prison separately.

Great World Manager Tang Jiapeng Suddenly Assassinated This Morning 134

Tang Was Shot Three Times in Vital Areas

He Died Shortly After Arriving at Baolong Hospital

丨丨An Innocent Passerby Was Killed by a Stray Bullet丨丨

At 1:00 AM this morning, an assassination occurred in front of the Great World on Avenue Edward VII, Tibet Road. The deceased was Tang Jiapeng, the manager of the Great World. The details are as follows:

Tang Jiapeng, a native of Ningbo, was 45 years old. He served as the manager of the Great World. He usually went to the Great World to handle matters every night and left around 1:00 AM the next morning. At 1:00 AM this morning, Tang walked out of the Great World, stepped into his Austin car. Just as he sat down and the driver had not yet started the car, gunshots suddenly came from behind the car, shooting into the car. More than ten shots were fired in total. Tang was shot three times, one shot entered from the back of his neck and came out of his chest, one shot entered from his right rib and came out of his left rib, and another shot injured his right leg. At that time, the visitors to the Great World had just dispersed, and the entrance was very crowded. Hearing the gunshots, the crowd scattered and fled. The staff inside the Great World heard the news and immediately took Tang to Baolong Hospital on Baker Road in the original car for treatment. Unfortunately, all the injuries were in vital areas, and the treatment was ineffective. He died shortly after arriving at the hospital. Also, when the stray bullets were flying, an innocent passerby was also seriously injured and died on the spot. This person was wearing a white short shirt and black pants. When the reporter received the news, he rushed to Baolong Hospital to inquire. Baker Road was full of cars, all of whom came to see the situation after hearing the news. The family members of Mr. Tang were crying and wailing, which was very tragic. Furthermore, as of 3:00 AM this morning, the Great World was still crowded with people. The pedestrian who was killed by the stray bullet was still lying in the corner of the wall, and the body had not been removed.

[P] Dr. Chen Cheng's Treatment of Rare Diseases is Miraculous

Dr. Chen Cheng, the medical director of Renji Hospital, is very experienced in medicine. Those who seek medical treatment from him will recover quickly. Recently, it was heard that a local man named Yang Gusheng, who is 42 years old, suffered from intestinal pain, and he would often faint and lose consciousness when the pain was severe. This has been going on for 18 years. Mr. Yang was destitute and unable to afford medical treatment. In early April of this year, he went to Renji Hospital and begged for a diagnosis. After examination by Dr. Chen, it was found that he had large intestine adhesion. He immediately performed surgery, removing 88 inches of decaying large and small intestines. After more than two months of treatment, he has now recovered and been discharged from the hospital. The doctor's surgery is miraculously effective, comparable to the ancient Yu Fu, which is admirable. It is also heard that when Mr. Yang entered the hospital, his body weight was only 92 pounds, but now it has increased to 120 pounds. Shanghai-Nanjing-Suzhou Tobacco and Alcohol Merchants Refuse to Pay Tobacco and Alcohol License Tax 136

They Appoint Six Representatives to Petition in Beijing to Abolish the Tax

The Shanghai-Nanjing-Suzhou Tobacco and Alcohol Industry Association has convened representatives in Shanghai to hold a joint meeting to oppose the tobacco and alcohol license tax and the newly formulated quota tax, and established the Joint Association of the Shanghai-Nanjing-Suzhou Tobacco and Alcohol Industry Association. It is now learned that the association has publicly appointed Jin Yunjie, Cao Gexian, Dai Zhuohou, Huang Yuming, Yu Xunlu, and Huang Wenqing to go to Beijing tomorrow to petition for the abolition of the tax, or to reduce the tax rate to reduce the burden. According to a committee member of the association, the tobacco and alcohol license tax has been increasing over the years, which is inconsistent with the regulations of the ministry. In addition, the collecting agencies are inconsistent, and the local wine for both tobacco and alcohol has already been taxed for production and sales. Cigarettes are also subject to a unified tax. The name of the license tax is actually redundant. Now, before the goal of the request is achieved, it has been decided to send the taxes that should be paid to the local chamber of commerce according to the original amount and level of the summer committee this year for temporary preservation, pending resolution. As for the newly established quota tax, the regulations are harsh and cumbersome, similar to the lijin. If implemented, there will be even more disputes. Therefore, the government should be requested to abolish it, and the Suzhou merchants are in trouble.

It Will Return to Shanghai Tomorrow Morning and Then Sail to Qingdao

Unemployed Workers Demand Placement

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Puan steamer, which operates the Putuo-Qingdao special route and is specially used for summer vacationers, set sail from the China Merchants North Wharf on Broadway Road at 5:00 PM yesterday for its first voyage to Putuo. The chief of the general affairs section agreed to place 15 people. When it was time to set sail yesterday, the Seamen's Union sent photos of the unemployed workers to the company for selection and employment, and ordered the workers to board the ship to wait for work. Temporarily, because it was not approved by the general manager and was not registered, they did not work on the ship. It is heard that the union is now rushing to complete the registration procedures so that they can wait for selection when the next shift sets sail.

The Fourth District of the County Conducts a Fly Eradication Campaign 140

丨More than 168,000 Flies Were Killed in Ten Days丨

During the summer season, epidemics are prevalent in the fourth district of the county, Sanlintang, Pudong. The district chief, Fu Dianying, believes that flies are the medium for the spread of various epidemics. In order to address the root cause, in addition to working with the local Public Security Bureau to rectify pits and toilets everywhere, he also convened the Farmers' Education Center, various schools, and social education institutions to organize a Fly Eradication Campaign Committee. Because the speed of fly reproduction is extremely alarming, killing a female fly in early summer can reduce tens of millions of flies. The committee formulated a plan and purchased a large number of fly swatters from the district office to distribute to various schools for use. They also sent letters to the district party department, the Public Security Bureau, and the heads of various townships, villages, and neighborhoods, urging them to work together to mobilize the entire population, organize groups to promote, and engage in fly eradication work. More than 168,000 flies were killed in ten days. The best results were achieved by Wuquan, Zuoxin, Xinmin, and San Schools, each of which killed about 30,000 flies. Those who excelled as individuals and groups were given prizes separately. The district is now immersing all the dead flies in kerosene for public incineration.

Letter Extortion Case: Police Request Handwriting Verification 144

Wu Ada's Handwriting is Neat

Verification Reveals Matching Numbers

Zhou Asi, Zhang Caigen (also known as A'er), Wu Ada, and others from Tongzhou, colluded with Zhang Weilin, who is at large. Starting from the 13th of last month to the 10th of this month, they repeatedly wrote threatening letters to Sun Yuanyou at 287 Zhaofeng Road, extorting 1,000 yuan. They sent a total of six letters, the last of which included a bullet, and was left near a telegraph pole at the corner of Zhoujiazu Road, covered with stones to avoid being seen. Sun reported this to the Huishan Police Station, which ordered detectives Wang Jinsheng and others to disguise themselves and arrest Zhou Asi and the other two. They were handed over to the First Special District Court for interrogation and detention, as previously reported in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, Judge Wu Zehan continued the trial in the Third Criminal Court. Police lawyer Zhang Tianyin stated that the case was adjourned. Defendant Zhou Asi confessed at the police station that he delivered the sixth threatening letter, but the idea originated with Zhang Caigen (who worked as a chauffeur for the victim's family), who discussed it with Zhang Weilin, who is at large, several times. Wu Ada was tasked with writing the six letters, but initially claimed he could not write. After repeated urging, he began to write the text, spanning three large sheets. He deliberately wrote neatly, and upon verification, some numbers matched. The police handwriting expert is currently out of town. The prosecution requests another adjournment to allow the court to have a handwriting expert confirm the writing. The three sheets written by Wu Ada were then submitted for inspection. The victim, Sun Yuanyou, testified that the first letter demanded 1,000 yuan in a peaceful tone, while the second letter threatened kidnapping with a ransom of 200,000 yuan if the demand was not met. The meeting locations were set at the end of North Sichuan Road and Zhoujiazu Road, but no one showed up to negotiate. When questioned, Zhou Asi's testimony was consistent with his police statement. Zhang Caigen and Wu Ada gave evasive answers, constantly shifting blame. Judge Wu ordered the defendants to be remanded in custody for further investigation at a later date.

Fire at Xiangyan Bridge, Zhabei 145

丨Hai Ning Egg Factory Warehouse on Fire丨

The refrigerated warehouse of York Company, located at No. 13 Xiangyan Bridge, Hujia Wooden Bridge, Zhabei, is owned by American merchant Maddison. It employs over eighty workers. The warehouse consists of eight buildings, with two southern rooms on the upper floor leased to Hai Ning Egg Factory, run by American merchant Haikesheng, as a warehouse. Yesterday morning around five o'clock, a fire suddenly broke out in the Hai Ning Egg Factory warehouse. At that time, it was just dawn, with few pedestrians. All the workers had already finished their shifts, so the fire went unnoticed. Only when the flames broke through the roof did nearby residents wake up from their dreams. They rushed to report to the Third Branch of the Fifth District, who informed the fire brigade. Fire trucks were dispatched to the scene to extinguish the fire. However, by then, the fire had spread from the upper floor to the lower refrigerated warehouse. Moreover, the contents of the refrigeration room were highly flammable, causing the fire to expand rapidly. The firefighters immediately focused on protecting the surrounding buildings while vigorously fighting the fire. It was not until around seven o'clock that the fire was completely extinguished. As a result, the York Company refrigerated warehouse and the Hai Ning Egg Factory warehouse were completely destroyed, resulting in significant losses. The cause of the fire has not yet been confirmed, but according to neighbors, it may have been caused by a worker dropping a cigarette while carrying goods into the egg factory warehouse.

A Dispute Over the Bride Waking Up Late 146

Why Must Madam Fu Jia Complain?

Another Lawsuit is Inevitable

Fu Maoyun, a resident of Xu Family Residence, Dongshouli, Yangjing Town, Pudong, is a farmer. He has a son named Qiusheng, 22 years old, who works as a shoemaker. In February of this year, he married the younger sister of Yu Miaolin from the neighborhood, and their relationship was very affectionate. However, Fu Miaosheng, a relative who lived in the same house and worked as a small wheel operator, and his wife, Madam Jia, constantly made sarcastic remarks about the bride waking up too late every morning. The bride was not willing to be outdone, and three days ago, they had a verbal altercation. The bride's eloquence was far superior to that of Madam Jia. After losing the verbal battle, Madam Jia told her husband. Miaosheng became even more enraged and gathered five thugs to come to the house and make trouble yesterday at 2 pm, while the bride's parents were out. The bride was terrified to see that one of them was carrying a handgun, so she fled out the back door and reported to the Second Precinct of the Third District. Miaosheng, finding no one in the house, smashed the dressing table and clock in the bridal chamber to pieces before fleeing. After the bride's father and others returned home, they were furious at the scene. They took photos of the damaged items and reported the incident to the police station, demanding that the perpetrators be arrested and investigated.

Women's Army Protests the Removal of Dung Pits 147

丨Demonstrating with Washing Pans and Bamboo Brooms丨

Xie Delin of Yancheng was recently commissioned by the Municipal Health and Finance Bureaus to handle sanitation matters in the Second Precinct of the Third District of Pudong. He established a sanitation station, with a trial period of one year to observe the results. It officially opened on the ninth of this month, and the first step was to remove private dung pits. However, these private pits were used by farmers for fertilizing their fields. The station's action was closely related to agricultural production. Therefore, the farmers united and protested. The day before yesterday afternoon, when the station's workers were removing pits along Sanjing Street, elderly women and children sounded copper alarms, gathering over a hundred people to cause trouble and prevent the work from proceeding. Many held washing pans and bamboo brooms in protest. A women's army created a formidable presence, appearing ready to use force. Fortunately, police and security team members arrived to quell the unrest, persuading the women to disperse and await a proper resolution.

They reluctantly appointed Yang Ziya, Yao Yuyuan, Chai Yiqing, Chen Huitang, and Ye Jufu as five representatives to petition, but there was no satisfactory outcome. Letter 159

Dear Chief Editor,

I am writing to you directly. I read a news item in the Shanghai news column of your newspaper on June 17 entitled "Grey Pill Organs Interrogation Record," which involves the names of several factories. I was shocked to read it. Sincerely, Nanyang Socks Factory General (South) Office, No. 5 Malu (Nanjing Road), June 17

Special Feature

Excerpt from Shenbao Series: On the Current State of Japan, Volume 1 162

Compiled by Chen Binhe, total of 214 pages

32mo paper, actual price 5 copper coins

This book is divided into three parts: translation, compilation, and rewriting;

Part One: "Research on Japanese History" is translated and compiled based on the "Materialist View of Japanese History" by the left-leaning Japanese scholar Sano Manabu. Although it only accounts for one-third of the original book in terms of volume, the essence of the original is preserved. The value of this book lies in its focus on the material production relations as the driving force of all social development, unlike the old Japanese historians who distorted history and focused solely on the deeds of heroes, prominent figures, and emperors, thus obscuring the great power of the working masses in history. The original author, Mr. Sano Manabu, was sentenced to life imprisonment by the Japanese authorities at the end of last year and is currently in prison. It is said that he came to Shanghai last year and was arrested by the Japanese police just as he was about to disembark. During interrogation at the Tokyo Police Department, he did not say a word, but only wrote six characters on a piece of paper: "A scholar can be killed, but not humiliated." Such a great personality deserves our respect.

Part Two: "Japan in the International Situation" is rewritten based on the materials in the first part of the 17th issue of the "World Economic Yearbook" by Varga (a Hungarian). (Published by the Japan Economic Criticism Society, Sōbun閣, July Showa 7). He is a world-renowned economist. His analysis of Japan in the international situation from an economic perspective is certainly very accurate.

Part Three: "The Expansion of Japan's Military Expenditure and Its Financial Crisis" is translated and compiled based on the materials in the second part of the 11th issue of the "Japan Economic Yearbook" published by the Toyo Keizai Shinposha (published in February Showa 8). This book is a relatively reliable source of economic information in the Japanese publishing industry. It does not shy away from the facts regarding the crisis of Japanese finance today and provides a detailed account, making it highly valuable for reference.

XXXXX 163

The editor, speaking of the necessity for our countrymen to study the Japanese question, explains in the preface:

"There is a Japanese story that says in ancient times there were two frogs, one living in a well in Kyoto and the other in a lotus pond in Osaka, forty miles apart. One day, they each set out from their home village, planning to explore the strange and unusual things of other places. They finally arrived at a place midway between Kyoto and Osaka, where they both stood firmly on their hind legs, gazing for the first time at the distant foreign land. Unfortunately, the frogs' eyes were located at the back of their heads, so their vision could only see what was behind them. Therefore, apart from seeing the scenery of their own hometowns, the two frogs saw nothing strange or unusual. So they returned to their respective places in a depressed mood. They imagined that Kyoto was a replica of Osaka, and Osaka was a replica of Kyoto. Until now, these two frogs still do not know and do not believe that there is a vast world outside the well and the lotus pond.

"There are similar analogies in ancient Chinese books,"

Zhuangzi writes, "A frog in a well cannot be talked to about the sea, because it is limited by its narrow space." The Biography of Ma Yuan in the Book of the Later Han also says, "Gongsun Shu was an emperor in Shu, and Yuan said to Gui Xiao, 'Ziyang is a frog at the bottom of a well.'" The frog mentioned here is of course used to describe people with narrow vision, self-imposed limitations, and complacency.

"As far as the situation in the last hundred years is concerned, our country may not be immune to the ridicule of being a 'frog in a well'. Although our country has become the target of political and economic aggression by Japanese imperialists, and a victim of Japanese imperialists' maritime and continental policies for decades, we still lack a fundamental understanding of our neighbor across the sea – a most ferocious imperialist. When observing our neighbor across the sea, some people, like those two frogs, are stubbornly using the eyes at the back of their heads to look, while others simply close their eyes and do not look. Therefore, some scholars and literati still hope to this day that our neighbor will quickly awaken and no longer resort to force; some hope that while resisting, there is still room for negotiation? Some offer advice to our neighbor, saying, "It is better to stop the 'total warfare' and instead use conquering our national spirit..."

"The situation in the Far East is becoming increasingly tense. Isn't it true that the environment no longer allows us to be 'frogs in a well'? Isn't it forcing us to move forward and use the eyes in front to become familiar with our neighbor across the sea?..."

XXXXX

Secondly, the editor's observation of the Sino-Japanese problem believes that there has been a major change in recent years, which is worthy of readers' attention. He said:

"Looking back on the past few years, I cannot say that I have made any research achievements or contributed anything to the country. I am ashamed of this. However, during this time, my observation of the Sino-Japanese problem has undergone a major change; that is, after returning from Japan in the seventeenth year, although on the one hand I was afraid of the thoroughness of Japanese research on various problems in our country, and on the other hand I felt the need for us to quickly study 'Japan', I still harbored the hope of close cooperation between China and Japan. It was not until after inspecting the Northeast in the winter of the nineteenth year that I realized that the Chinese nation, under the aggressive policy of Japanese imperialists, had no way out unless it unfolded the banner of national revolution. All those who loudly advocate 'Sino-Japanese friendship', 'coexistence and co-prosperity', and 'compromise' and 'peace' are just 'frogs in a well'. The outbreak of the September 18th Incident further confirmed the correctness of this observation. Therefore, if we cannot clearly recognize the aggressive policy of Japanese imperialism, we are not worthy of studying Japan, not worthy of being enemies of Japanese imperialism, but can only be slaves of Japanese imperialism. But at the same time, from observing the ideological turmoil within Japan in recent years, we can also see that Japanese imperialism is heading towards its downfall, and a new Japan is coming soon! We are convinced that the Japanese working masses, the every cell that creates a new Japan, will soon bear the new tasks of the new era."

Important Education News

Zhejiang Province's Education and Culture Expenditure for the 22nd Year 165

Totaling 2,116,000

The estimated education and culture expenditure for Zhejiang Province in the 22nd year, which was previously prepared by the Department of Education and submitted to the Department of Finance for compilation, totaled over 2,116,000 yuan. This is an increase of over 100,300 yuan, twice the amount of the tightened budget for the second half of last year. The Department of Education recently prepared this budget, with existing projects still based on the tightened standards of the second half of the 21st year. New projects, such as the new agricultural vocational schools and rural normal schools added in the 22nd year, as well as the examination fees and national military training committee expenses for graduates held by order, and national defense lecture fees, are also included. In practice, compared with the tightened amount of the previous year, there is no increase.

Procedures for Sending Students to the United States by Tsinghua 166

|Qualifications stipulated by the Ministry of Education|

25 students to be recruited through open examinations in Peiping

(Nanjing, 17th dispatch) The Ministry of Education has ordered Tsinghua University to openly select and send 25 government-funded students to the United States in the 22nd year, to be carefully handled by the school's examination committee. The Ministry has also ordered the issuance of a summary of the examination procedures: 1. Qualifications for applicants: A. Graduates of public or registered private colleges or above at home and abroad who have continued to study their subjects in graduate school for more than two years and have valuable specialized works or other achievements; B. Graduates of public or registered private colleges or above at home and abroad who have served in technical positions related to their subjects for more than two years; C. Graduates of public or registered private universities or independent colleges at home and abroad with excellent grades; 2. Applicants should apply for the following academic fields, and the distribution of the number of students admitted is as follows: Applied Optics 1, Applied Geophysics 1, Instrument and Vacuum Tube Manufacturing 2, National Defense Chemistry 2, Nitric Acid Manufacturing 1, Sulfuric Acid Manufacturing 1, Steel and Metallurgy 1, Aircraft Manufacturing 3, Ordnance 2, Refining 1, Water Conservancy and Hydropower Engineering 1, Crop Breeding 1, Veterinary Medicine 1, Plant Pathology 1, Soil Fertilizer 1, Statistics 1, International Finance and Trade 1, Public Administration 1; 3. The examination period will begin on August 10th and will be held separately in Peiping and Beijing; 4. The Examination Committee will be composed of the following nine members: 1. Three professors from Tsinghua University, 2. Four experts from other schools, 3. One representative sent by the Ministry, 4. The President of Tsinghua University will be the ex officio Chairman.

Joint Graduation Examination for Primary and Secondary Schools in Anhui Province 168

To be held in districts starting from July 1st

Since Yang Lianji became the head of the Department of Education of Anhui Province, he has attached great importance to the examination system. Therefore, the three matters of the joint graduation examination for primary and secondary schools in the province, the preliminary examination for recruits of the Central Military Academy, and the qualification examination for senior and ordinary civil servants have been actively prepared and carried out by Yang since he took office. In addition to the preliminary examination for recruits of the Central Military Academy, which began its first test yesterday, the joint graduation examination for primary and secondary schools is scheduled to be held simultaneously in districts starting from July 1st. Yesterday (the 15th), the Department issued a notice to all schools and bureaus, explaining the significance of the joint examination for primary and secondary schools and encouraging students throughout the province to pay attention to preparation. Jiangsu Department of Education Emphasizes the Appointment and Dismissal of Middle School Principals and Teachers 171

Zhou Fohai, the Director of the Department of Education of Jiangsu Province, has always adhered to the principle of seeking qualitative improvement in secondary education in this province. In addition to promulgating the measures for integrating teaching and discipline and raising the level of middle schools, he has now ordered all responsible personnel, as the semester is coming to an end, to eliminate personal feelings and attach importance to teaching and discipline in the appointment and dismissal of principals and teachers of various schools. The original orders are recorded as follows:

Order 1: It is hereby ordered that the principal of each county-run secondary school is in charge of the school's affairs, and his position is of great importance. If the selection is not correct, it will cause disputes in the whole school and delay the studies of young people. The director of the bureau is in charge of the educational administration of the whole county and is directly responsible for supervising the principals of the secondary schools. He should usually conduct thorough investigations. At the end of the year, he should review the past achievements of the principals in detail and carefully examine them to determine whether to stay or leave. Those who are derelict in their duties should eliminate personal feelings and apply for replacement to emphasize education. The selection of the successor should be cautious, not based on personal opinions, and not controlled by factions, so as to be fair and avoid disputes. In addition to separate orders, this order is urgently issued for the director of the bureau to comply with. This order.

Order 2: Although the selection and employment of teachers and staff in provincial schools has been carried out in accordance with regulations, whether the teaching is legal and whether the service is dutiful after the teachers and staff arrive at the school depends entirely on the principal's careful investigation, judging their merits and demerits, and observing their diligence and laziness as a basis for promotion and demotion. Now that the semester is coming to an end and teachers and staff are being re-hired, if there are teachers and staff in the school who are incompetent or not very responsible, they should be replaced and re-hired, without indulging the feelings of a few people and delaying the studies of many young people. Teachers who are knowledgeable but not responsible for disciplining students, or who are diligent at the beginning but lazy at the end, should also be dismissed to comply with the purpose of integrating teaching and discipline in this department. In addition to separate orders, this order is hereby issued for the principal of the school to comply with. This order.

Disputes Arise at the Middle School Joint Examination on the Third Day 178

Director Pan of the Department of Education issues a statement

The Municipal Education Bureau, following the order of the Ministry of Education, is holding a joint graduation examination for primary and secondary schools throughout the city. The middle school part, which has been held in twelve examination halls since the 15th, has been reported in the previous newspaper. Yesterday was the third day of the middle school joint examination. Unfortunately, disturbances occurred at the first examination hall (Daxia) and the third examination hall (Meizhuan) of the high school. The Education Bureau issued a temporary announcement, suspending the examination in the afternoon in order to investigate thoroughly. It is heard that a meeting of the Joint Examination Committee will be convened today to decide on the date and continue the examination. Regarding this matter, Director Pan of the Municipal Education Bureau issued the following statement:

The Municipal Education Bureau is holding this joint examination because it is related to national government orders. I have always adhered to two principles: 1. To be strict and thorough in advance; 2. To be extremely open in the results. Therefore, the appointment of members and examiners has been carefully selected, and the confidentiality of the test questions and printing has been strived for. I can say that I have nothing to be ashamed of. However, there have been many criticisms from the outside world regarding the joint examination method. Before the examination, students from other places came to Shanghai to incite opposition, leading to repeated calls for strikes and boycotts. Fortunately, after negotiations and precautions, nothing happened. Unexpectedly, it was discovered yesterday morning that the composition topic of the high school English subject seemed to have been found out by a small number of students outside. Regardless of whether it is true or not, it must be thoroughly investigated. I immediately sent someone to investigate secretly, and at the same time telephoned the examination halls to temporarily change the two English composition topics. The second examination hall (Shanghai University) and the fourth examination hall (Shanghai Middle School) of the high school followed suit. Unexpectedly, the students in the first and third examination halls were incited by a small number of students with other motives, and the order was disrupted. Students were sent out to incite others, resulting in disturbances in the seventh examination hall of the junior high school of Minli Middle School. At that time, I immediately notified all examination halls that the history and biology subjects for high school in the afternoon, and the history subject for junior high school, could be suspended for the sake of prudence and prevention of fraud. If there was good order, the order should still be maintained, and no other accidents occurred. At present, in the first examination hall (Chengzhong) and the eighth examination hall (Qingxin Girls' Middle School) of the junior high school, all the students participating in the joint examination have completed all the examination items as usual. Other junior high school students are only missing the history subject, and the students with the worst order and the most violent incitement are only from two or three schools, and clues have been found. At 3:00 p.m. today (yesterday), student representatives from Daxia Middle School convened a meeting of student representatives from some middle schools in the school. After 5:00 p.m., more than 100 people gathered and went to the Education Bureau to petition. I sent Commissioner Jiang to meet them and told them three points: 1. The Education Bureau will definitely investigate this matter thoroughly and strictly. Once it is found out, no matter what, it will be punished according to law. 2. The subjects of the middle school joint examination have not been completed. After the Joint Examination Committee identifies a proper method, all unexamined subjects should be continued in accordance with the revised method. 3. If the Education Bureau has organized a joint examination with complete fraud, it will naturally listen to the investigation and handling of the municipal government and the Ministry of Education. The students then dispersed. In short, the joint examination system was originally a new one. I, as the head of the Education Bureau, was ordered to prepare it and tried my best to be cautious. Fortunately, the committee members assisted in the examination with their voluntary hard work, which is very grateful. However, this unfortunate incident occurred in the midst of a hundred precautions, and a small number of students took the opportunity to incite trouble. I feel deeply ashamed of all parties. In addition to separately reporting to the Ministry of Education and the Municipal Government and asking for punishment for my dereliction of duty, the joint examination must continue to be carried out strictly. As for any unscrupulous officials who leak the test questions, once they are thoroughly investigated and confirmed, they will be severely punished. However, students who intend to oppose the joint examination, make trouble under the pretext, or have other backgrounds and vainly hope to expand the situation should still be strictly stopped. It is hoped that the principals and teachers of all middle schools will share the responsibility and guide the students on the right track, which is not only a blessing for one person. Some people say that this joint examination is too strict. Students who fail three subjects must repeat the grade, and those who fail one or two subjects must take a make-up examination. If they fail the make-up examination, they cannot be promoted, which inevitably makes students feel difficult. Regarding this point, for the sake of the young people's time, it seems that there is a need for consideration. In my humble opinion, in addition to the main subjects, those who fail three subjects must repeat the grade, and those who fail one or two subjects in the make-up examination should be given special leniency to allow them to temporarily advance to school as special students and re-enter as regular students after passing the make-up examination in the next joint examination, so that both the meaning of the joint examination and the young people's time are taken care of. The Education Bureau submitted a document to the Ministry of Education earlier last month requesting this, and yesterday it received a request for leniency from the principals of various middle schools, which will be forwarded to the Ministry of Education for instructions immediately. The primary school joint examination is still scheduled to be held on the 19th and 20th, and will not be changed.

According to Riri News, since the middle school graduation joint examination was held, yesterday was the third day. Unfortunately, disturbances occurred successively in the two examination halls of Daxia and Meizhuan on this day. The disturbances in Meizhuan seemed not as severe as those in Daxia. A Riri News reporter made a special trip to Daxia Middle School yesterday to inquire about the truth. According to a middle school student taking the joint examination, some people discovered that students from Jianguo Middle School submitted test papers with more than 20 questions within ten minutes, which has aroused suspicion. At the end of the examination on the afternoon of the second day, someone found mimeographed question papers in the examination hall, which were English test questions, "China after Ten Years." On the morning of the third day, the chief examiner Du Gang arrived and issued the topic, which was the same as the mimeographed question paper. The students taking the joint examination immediately became chaotic and questioned Du. Du immediately wrote a notice in white paper with red characters, saying, "It is unfortunate that there has been fraud in the English subject. All English examinations in each examination room should be stopped immediately. Report to the committee chairman for thorough investigation and handling. Notify the students to maintain order." And personally signed by Du. After this incident occurred, some students reported to Mayor Wu by telephone, asking the mayor to come to the school, but no municipal government personnel came until the evening. At that time, the students regarded the mimeographed question paper obtained in advance as important evidence of fraud, so they asked Du to sign it as a letter, and Du also complied. It is found that among the middle schools taking the joint examination in Daxia yesterday, there were students from Daxia, Guanghua, Jianguo, Zhongxi Girls' School, Zhiren Yong, Peiming, Shanghai, China, Huaguo, Guangnan Yang, Model, and Fudan Affiliated Middle School. In addition to this mimeographed question paper, many pieces of paper scattered on the ground were also obtained. After piecing together the pieces of paper one by one, they were also words for filling in sentences. Yesterday afternoon, all middle schools in Shanghai sent student representatives, originally planning to hold a general assembly of middle school student representatives in the classroom of Daxia Middle School, but it was temporarily stopped by the police sent by the Public Security Bureau. The student representatives from each middle school are now secretly discussing and deliberating the method, and the Riri News reporter repeatedly inquired about the meeting place, but they refused to tell. The spokesman also said that when the students became chaotic, Du said that he could change the topic and write it on the blackboard, but the students insisted that they did not want to take the joint examination, so this line of mediation was not expected to be realized.

Chen Chuanzhang Wins Welton Cup Tennis Final 196

Three Straight Wins Against Hu Qichang

The Welton Cup tennis final of Aurora University was held yesterday. Chen Chuanzhang defeated Hu Qichang in three straight sets to win the championship. The scores were 6-3, 6-3, and 6-4. A large crowd watched.

Chen and Hu's skills: Chen's shots are harder and more powerful. Several forehand smashes were very exciting. The smash is also okay, but the backhand lacks grip. There are many double faults in the serve. Chen is always in an offensive position throughout the game. Hu Qichang's work is okay, but weakness is his biggest problem. The chop is very effective, but his ball is weak and cannot kill people. The number of wild balls that go out of bounds is uncountable.

Match situation Chen won the first game as soon as he served. After 2-2 and 3-3, Chen won three consecutive games and won the first set 6-3. After each of the second set, Chen took a very advantageous lead of 4-1. Hu fought to 3-4, but still failed 3-6. In the last set, Hu Qichang seemed to be revitalized. 3-0 won three consecutive games. However, Chen immediately won back four games and finished the game 6-4.

Special Article

General Situation of Jinan University in the Year After the War 199

㈢ (Chen Qiying)

㈣ General Situation of Administrative Facilities

The Secretariat is the highest authority in the school's administrative affairs. Previously, there were two sections: General Affairs and Registration. The General Affairs Section had documentation, general affairs, printing, medical, and accounting and cashiering groups to handle the affairs under its jurisdiction. The Registration Section was dedicated to handling the resolutions made by the Academic Affairs Meeting, and was responsible for the implementation of academic affairs. Recently, the Registration Section was transferred to the Academic Affairs Committee, and the General Affairs Section was abolished. The original documentation, general affairs, printing, medical (renamed health), and accounting and cashiering groups were expanded into sections to clarify the authority of academic and general affairs and to make the handling procedures more convenient. However, the school's funds have always been extremely tight. The monthly administrative expenses are only more than 5,000 taels, including special, equipment, and experimental expenses. It is naturally difficult to handle affairs, but in the face of difficulties, we try our best to economize and find ways to make things progress gradually. This is due to the effective guidance of the responsible personnel. The current Secretary-General is still Mr. Yang Yufen, and the secretaries are Mr. Zeng Ke Duan and Mr. Bao Shou Kang. The section chiefs of the documentation, general affairs, printing, and health sections are still Mr. Chen Zhongfu, Mr. Bao Shou Kang concurrently, Mr. Chen Qiying and Mr. Tang Feili, and the accounting and cashiering sections are still handled by accountants Xi Yushu and Wang Haifan. The following is a brief description of the important matters handled by each section in the past year.

In terms of documentation, although there are not many staff members, the documents handled through division of labor and cooperation have been quite remarkable. Although the school's regulations are reviewed and revised by the Legal Committee, the Documentation Section is still responsible for collecting and drafting them. The compilation of the list of 21 and 22 years and the organization of archives have all achieved considerable results.

In terms of general affairs, general affairs is the most difficult thing to handle in school administration. The general affairs of our school is particularly difficult due to the difficulty of funding. Only with proper management can we achieve results. For the convenience of work, it is divided into several parts

1. Engineering, since the 128 War, in addition to the important repair projects handled by the post-war consolidation committee, other projects are handled by the engineering. The construction of the school's roads, the cultivation of flowers, the reconstruction of toilets, and the renovation of bathrooms have all achieved very significant results. As for the school's electricity, it was previously supplied by the Zhabei Electric Light Company, which cost more than 1,000 yuan per month, which was not economical. In particular, we strived to conserve other consumption during the summer vacation last year, and operated our own electric light factory, which cost only more than 400 yuan per month including fuel and labor. Because our school is located in a remote township, all drinks must be self-sufficient, so we have self-flowing well equipment, but all the machines and water pipes were destroyed by the enemy during the Shanghai War, so we bought another 10-horsepower diesel engine, and the water pumped out was tested by the Municipal Health Bureau and was extremely hygienic. Also, because the school's area is wide and the various parts are far apart, it is extremely inconvenient to contact each other in case of an accident. The previous telephone was only for external calls, but now all parts of the school are equipped with extensions to save the time of contact and improve the efficiency of handling. 2. Service, the management of all workers in the school is subject to various regulations, which are strictly implemented, and all workers in the school wear uniforms and badges, which are not only neat and tidy on the surface, but also easy to check in practice. As for the treatment of workers, it has been effectively improved, the monthly wages are cleared in advance, and workers' night schools are set up to train them to increase their knowledge and working ability.

3. Purchase, in order to promote domestic goods, all items purchased by general affairs are used as domestic goods as much as possible, and foreign goods are used only when there are no suitable substitutes among domestic goods, and enemy goods are absolutely not used. As for the accounts of various merchants, they are settled monthly and never in arrears.

In addition, the receiving, receiving, and storage departments all follow the regulations, the handling procedures are convenient, and the assessment is simple.
